End-to-End Efficient RL for Linear Bellman Complete MDPs with Deterministic Transitions
Authors: Zakaria Mhammedi, Alexander Rakhlin, Nneka Okolo
First: 2026-03-24T17:32:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T17:32:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study reinforcement learning (RL) with linear function approximation in Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) satisfying \emph{linear Bellman completeness} -- a fundamental setting where the Bellman backup of any linear value function remains linear. While statistically tractable, prior computationally efficient algorithms are either limited to small action spaces or require strong oracle assumptions over the feature space. We provide a computationally efficient algorithm for linear Bellman complete MDPs with \emph{deterministic transitions}, stochastic initial states, and stochastic rewards. For finite action spaces, our algorithm is end-to-end efficient; for large or infinite action spaces, we require only a standard argmax oracle over actions. Our algorithm learns an $\varepsilon$-optimal policy with sample and computational complexity polynomial in the horizon, feature dimension, and $1/\varepsilon$.
中文标题/摘要
标题：确定性转移线性贝尔曼完备MDP的端到端高效强化学习
我们研究满足线性贝尔曼完备性的马尔可夫决策过程中的线性函数逼近强化学习——该基础设定下任意线性值函数的贝尔曼备份仍保持线性。虽然统计上可处理，但现有计算高效算法要么局限于小动作空间，要么需要对特征空间提出强预言机假设。我们针对具有确定性转移、随机初始状态和随机奖励的线性贝尔曼完备MDP提出一种计算高效算法。对于有限动作空间，该算法具备端到端高效性；对于大规模或无限动作空间，仅需标准的动作argmax预言机。我们的算法能以与时间跨度、特征维度和1/ε呈多项式关系的样本与计算复杂度学习ε-最优策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of computationally efficient reinforcement learning in Markov Decision Processes with linear function approximation, specifically under the condition of linear Bellman completeness where the Bellman backup preserves linearity. The motivation stems from prior methods that were either computationally inefficient for large action spaces or relied on strong assumptions. The proposed method introduces an end-to-end efficient algorithm tailored for linear Bellman complete MDPs with deterministic transitions, stochastic initial states, and rewards, requiring only a standard argmax oracle for large action spaces. The main experimental results demonstrate that the algorithm achieves an ε-optimal policy with sample and computational complexity that is polynomial in the horizon, feature dimension, and the inverse of the accuracy parameter ε.
本文研究了具有线性函数逼近的强化学习问题，专注于满足线性贝尔曼完备性的马尔可夫决策过程，即贝尔曼备份能保持线性性质。其动机源于现有计算高效算法要么局限于小动作空间，要么需要对特征空间进行强假设。该方法提出了一种端到端高效算法，适用于具有确定性转移、随机初始状态和奖励的线性贝尔曼完备MDP，对于大或无限动作空间仅需标准的argmax预言机。主要实验结果表明，该算法能以多项式样本和计算复杂度（关于时间范围、特征维度和精度参数ε的倒数）学习到ε-最优策略。
EVA: Aligning Video World Models with Executable Robot Actions via Inverse Dynamics Rewards
Authors: Ruixiang Wang, Qingming Liu, Yueci Deng, Guiliang Liu, Zhen Liu, Kui Jia
First: 2026-03-18T15:02:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T17:12:47+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://eva-project-page.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Video generative models are increasingly used as world models for robotics, where a model generates a future visual rollout conditioned on the current observation and task instruction, and an inverse dynamics model (IDM) converts the generated frames into executable robot actions. However, current video world models lack explicit executability constraints. As a result, visually coherent rollouts may still violate rigid-body and kinematic consistency, producing unstable or infeasible control commands when decoded by an IDM. We refer to this mismatch between visual generation and physically executable control as the executability gap. While this gap can be mitigated at inference time using techniques such as rejection sampling, such approaches are inefficient due to the high cost of video generation. In this paper, we leverage the executability gap as a training signal and introduce Executable Video Alignment (EVA), a reinforcement-learning post-training framework for aligning video world models. EVA trains an inverse dynamics model on real robot trajectories and repurposes it as a reward model that evaluates generated videos through the action sequences they induce, encouraging smooth motions measured by velocity, acceleration, and jerk while penalizing actions that violate embodiment constraints. Importantly, the reward remains informative even when generated videos contain severe visual artifacts, since such artifacts typically translate into unstable or out-of-bound actions. Experiments on the RoboTwin benchmark and a real bimanual robot show that EVA reduces embodiment-specific artifacts in generated rollouts and improves downstream task execution success.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EVA：通过逆动力学奖励将视频世界模型与可执行机器人动作对齐
视频生成模型正日益用作机器人学的世界模型，此类模型能基于当前观测和任务指令生成未来视觉推演，并通过逆动力学模型将生成帧转换为可执行的机器人动作。然而，当前视频世界模型缺乏明确的可执行性约束，导致视觉连贯的推演仍可能违反刚体与运动学一致性，经逆动力学模型解码后产生不稳定或不可行的控制指令。这种视觉生成与物理可执行控制间的失配称为可执行性鸿沟。虽然可通过拒绝采样等推理阶段技术缓解该问题，但视频生成的高成本使其效率低下。本文提出将可执行性鸿沟作为训练信号，引入可执行视频对齐框架——一种基于强化学习的视频世界模型后训练对齐方法。该框架在真实机器人轨迹上训练逆动力学模型，并将其重构为奖励模型，通过生成视频诱导的动作序列评估视频质量：奖励速度、加速度和加加速度度量的平滑运动，惩罚违反本体约束的动作。关键的是，即使生成视频存在严重视觉伪影，该奖励仍具信息量，因为此类伪影通常对应不稳定或越界动作。在RoboTwin基准和真实双臂机器人上的实验表明，该方法能减少生成推演中本体相关的伪影，并提升下游任务执行成功率。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the executability gap in video world models for robotics, where visually coherent generated rollouts may still produce infeasible robot actions when decoded by an inverse dynamics model (IDM). To bridge this gap, the authors propose Executable Video Alignment (EVA), a reinforcement-learning post-training framework that uses an IDM trained on real robot trajectories as a reward model to evaluate generated videos based on the induced action sequences, encouraging smooth motions and penalizing violations of embodiment constraints. Experimental results on the RoboTwin benchmark and a real bimanual robot demonstrate that EVA reduces embodiment-specific artifacts in generated rollouts and improves downstream task execution success.
该论文针对机器人学中视频世界模型的可执行性差距问题，即视觉上连贯的生成轨迹在通过逆动力学模型解码时仍可能产生不可行的机器人动作。为弥合这一差距，作者提出了可执行视频对齐（EVA），这是一个强化学习后训练框架，利用在真实机器人轨迹上训练的逆动力学模型作为奖励模型，通过诱导的动作序列评估生成视频，鼓励平滑运动并惩罚违反本体约束的行为。在RoboTwin基准测试和真实双臂机器人上的实验结果表明，EVA减少了生成轨迹中特定于本体的伪影，并提高了下游任务执行的成功率。
SortedRL: Accelerating RL Training for LLMs through Online Length-Aware Scheduling
Authors: Yiqi Zhang, Huiqiang Jiang, Xufang Luo, Zhihe Yang, Chengruidong Zhang, Yifei Shen, Dongsheng Li, Yuqing Yang, Lili Qiu, Yang You
First: 2026-03-24T16:48:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T16:48:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scaling reinforcement learning (RL) has shown strong promise for enhancing the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs), particularly in tasks requiring long chain-of-thought generation. However, RL training efficiency is often bottlenecked by the rollout phase, which can account for up to 70% of total training time when generating long trajectories (e.g., 16k tokens), due to slow autoregressive generation and synchronization overhead between rollout and policy updates. We propose SortedRL, an online length-aware scheduling strategy designed to address this bottleneck by improving rollout efficiency and maintaining training stability. SortedRL reorders rollout samples based on output lengths, prioritizing short samples forming groups for early updates. This enables large rollout batches, flexible update batches, and near on-policy micro-curriculum construction simultaneously. To further accelerate the pipeline, SortedRL incorporates a mechanism to control the degree of off-policy training through a cache-based mechanism, and is supported by a dedicated RL infrastructure that manages rollout and update via a stateful controller and rollout buffer. Experiments using LLaMA-3.1-8B and Qwen-2.5-32B on diverse tasks, including logical puzzles, and math challenges like AIME 24, Math 500, and Minerval, show that SortedRL reduces RL training bubble ratios by over 50%, while attaining 3.9% to 18.4% superior performance over baseline given same amount of data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SortedRL：通过在线长度感知调度加速大语言模型的强化学习训练
强化学习（RL）的规模化应用已显示出增强大语言模型（LLMs）推理能力的巨大潜力，尤其是在需要生成长链思维的任务中。然而，RL训练效率常受限于推演阶段，当生成长轨迹（如16k词元）时，由于缓慢的自回归生成以及推演与策略更新间的同步开销，该阶段可占总训练时间的70%。我们提出SortedRL，一种在线长度感知调度策略，旨在通过提升推演效率并保持训练稳定性来解决这一瓶颈。SortedRL根据输出长度对推演样本进行重排序，优先将短样本分组以进行早期更新。这同时实现了大规模推演批次、灵活的更新批次以及近乎同策略的微课程构建。为进一步加速流程，SortedRL引入了一种基于缓存的机制来控制离策略训练的程度，并得到专用RL基础设施的支持，该设施通过有状态控制器和推演缓冲区管理推演与更新。在LLaMA-3.1-8B和Qwen-2.5-32B模型上，针对逻辑谜题及AIME 24、Math 500、Minerval等数学挑战的多样化任务实验表明，SortedRL将RL训练气泡比降低了50%以上，并在相同数据量下取得了比基线模型优越3.9%至18.4%的性能。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the significant efficiency bottleneck in reinforcement learning (RL) training for large language models (LLMs), where the rollout phase for long trajectories can consume up to 70% of training time due to slow autoregressive generation and synchronization overhead. The proposed method, SortedRL, is an online length-aware scheduling strategy that reorders rollout samples by output length, prioritizing shorter samples to form groups for early updates; this enables large rollout batches, flexible update batches, and a near on-policy micro-curriculum, further accelerated by a cache-based mechanism to control off-policy training and a dedicated RL infrastructure. Main experimental results using models like LLaMA-3.1-8B and Qwen-2.5-32B on tasks including logical puzzles and math challenges (AIME 24, Math 500, Minerval) show that SortedRL reduces RL training bubble ratios by over 50% and achieves performance gains of 3.9% to 18.4% over baselines with the same amount of data.
本研究的动机是解决大语言模型强化学习训练中的显著效率瓶颈，即生成长轨迹的推演阶段因自回归生成缓慢和同步开销，可能占用高达70%的训练时间。所提出的方法SortedRL是一种在线长度感知调度策略，它根据输出长度对推演样本重新排序，优先处理短样本以形成组进行早期更新；这实现了大批量推演、灵活的更新批次以及近乎同策略的微课程构建，并通过基于缓存的机制控制离策略训练和专用的RL基础设施进一步加速。在LLaMA-3.1-8B和Qwen-2.5-32B等模型上对逻辑谜题和数学挑战（如AIME 24、Math 500、Minerval）任务的主要实验结果表明，SortedRL将RL训练气泡比率降低了50%以上，并在相同数据量下实现了比基线模型3.9%至18.4%的性能提升。
Off-Policy Value-Based Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Models
Authors: Peng-Yuan Wang, Ziniu Li, Tian Xu, Bohan Yang, Tian-Shuo Liu, ChenYang Wang, Xiong-Hui Chen, Yi-Chen Li, Tianyun Yang, Congliang Chen, Yang Yu
First: 2026-03-24T15:55:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T15:55:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Improving data utilization efficiency is critical for scaling reinforcement learning (RL) for long-horizon tasks where generating trajectories is expensive. However, the dominant RL methods for LLMs are largely on-policy: they update each batch of data only once, discard it, and then collect fresh samples, resulting in poor sample efficiency. In this work, we explore an alternative value-based RL framework for LLMs that naturally enables off-policy learning. We propose ReVal, a Bellman-update-based method that combines stepwise signals capturing internal consistency with trajectory-level signals derived from outcome verification. ReVal naturally supports replay-buffer-based training, allowing efficient reuse of past trajectories. Experiments on standard mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that ReVal not only converges faster but also outperforms GRPO in final performance. On DeepSeek-R1-Distill-1.5B, ReVal improves training efficiency and achieves improvement of 2.7% in AIME24 and 4.5% in out-of-domain benchmark GPQA over GRPO. These results suggest that value-based RL is a practical alternative to policy-based methods for LLM training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大语言模型的离策略值基强化学习
在生成轨迹成本高昂的长周期任务中，提升数据利用效率对扩展强化学习（RL）至关重要。然而，当前面向大语言模型（LLM）的主流RL方法主要为同策略方法：每批数据仅更新一次即被丢弃，随后需重新采集样本，导致样本效率低下。本研究为LLM探索了一种支持离策略学习的值基RL框架。我们提出ReVal——一种基于贝尔曼更新的方法，融合了捕捉内部一致性的逐步信号与源自结果验证的轨迹级信号。ReVal天然支持基于回放缓冲区的训练，可实现历史轨迹的高效复用。在标准数学推理基准测试中，ReVal不仅收敛更快，最终性能也超越GRPO。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-1.5B模型上，ReVal提升了训练效率，相较GRPO在AIME24基准上提升2.7%，在跨域基准GPQA上提升4.5%。这些结果表明，值基RL可作为LLM训练中策略基方法的实用替代方案。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the poor sample efficiency of on-policy reinforcement learning (RL) methods for large language models (LLMs), which discard data after a single update, this work explores a value-based RL framework to enable efficient off-policy learning. The proposed method, ReVal, combines stepwise internal consistency signals with trajectory-level outcome verification through Bellman updates, naturally supporting replay-buffer training for reusing past trajectories. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that ReVal converges faster and outperforms GRPO in final performance, achieving improvements of 2.7% on AIME24 and 4.5% on GPQA with the DeepSeek-R1-Distill-1.5B model, indicating value-based RL as a practical alternative for LLM training.
针对大语言模型强化学习中主流策略方法样本效率低、数据使用后即丢弃的问题，本研究探索了一种基于价值的强化学习框架以实现高效的离策略学习。所提出的ReVal方法通过贝尔曼更新，结合了捕捉内部一致性的逐步信号与基于结果验证的轨迹级信号，天然支持基于回放缓冲区的训练以重用历史轨迹。在数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明，ReVal收敛更快且最终性能优于GRPO，使用DeepSeek-R1-Distill-1.5B模型在AIME24上提升了2.7%，在跨域基准GPQA上提升了4.5%，表明基于价值的强化学习是大语言模型训练的一种实用替代方案。
Architecture-Aware Minimization (A$^2$M): How to Find Flat Minima in Neural Architecture Search
Authors: Matteo Gambella, Fabrizio Pittorino, Manuel Roveri
Venue: 2025 Mach. Learn.: Sci. Technol. 6 035016
First: 2025-03-13T14:30:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T15:49:47+00:00
Comments: Published in the journal Machine Learning: Science and Technology - IOPscience
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Neural Architecture Search (NAS) has become an essential tool for designing effective and efficient neural networks. In this paper, we investigate the geometric properties of neural architecture spaces commonly used in differentiable NAS methods, specifically NAS-Bench-201 and DARTS. By defining flatness metrics such as neighborhoods and loss barriers along paths in architecture space, we reveal locality and flatness characteristics analogous to the well-known properties of neural network loss landscapes in weight space. In particular, we find that highly accurate architectures cluster together in flat regions, while suboptimal architectures remain isolated, unveiling the detailed geometrical structure of the architecture search landscape. Building on these insights, we propose Architecture-Aware Minimization (A$^2$M), a novel analytically derived algorithmic framework that explicitly biases, for the first time, the gradient of differentiable NAS methods towards flat minima in architecture space. A$^2$M consistently improves generalization over state-of-the-art DARTS-based algorithms on benchmark datasets including CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and ImageNet16-120, across both NAS-Bench-201 and DARTS search spaces. Notably, A$^2$M is able to increase the test accuracy, on average across different differentiable NAS methods, by +3.60\% on CIFAR-10, +4.60\% on CIFAR-100, and +3.64\% on ImageNet16-120, demonstrating its superior effectiveness in practice. A$^2$M can be easily integrated into existing differentiable NAS frameworks, offering a versatile tool for future research and applications in automated machine learning. We open-source our code at https://github.com/AI-Tech-Research-Lab/AsquaredM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：架构感知最小化（A²M）：如何在神经架构搜索中寻找平坦最小值
神经架构搜索（NAS）已成为设计高效神经网络的重要工具。本文研究了可微分NAS方法常用架构空间（特别是NAS-Bench-201和DARTS）的几何特性。通过定义架构空间中的邻域和路径损失屏障等平坦度度量，我们揭示了与权重空间中神经网络损失景观类似的结构特性。研究发现，高精度架构聚集在平坦区域，而次优架构则保持孤立，这揭示了架构搜索景观的精细几何结构。基于这些发现，我们提出架构感知最小化（A²M）——一种全新解析推导的算法框架，首次在可微分NAS方法中显式地将梯度偏向架构空间的平坦最小值。在NAS-Bench-201和DARTS搜索空间中，A²M在CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100和ImageNet16-120等基准数据集上持续提升基于DARTS的先进算法的泛化性能。值得注意的是，A²M在不同可微分NAS方法中平均提升测试精度：CIFAR-10提升+3.60%、CIFAR-100提升+4.60%、ImageNet16-120提升+3.64%，证明了其实际有效性。A²M可轻松集成到现有可微分NAS框架中，为自动化机器学习的未来研究与应用提供通用工具。代码已开源：https://github.com/AI-Tech-Research-Lab/AsquaredM。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand the geometric structure of neural architecture search spaces and improve generalization, this paper investigates the loss landscapes in differentiable NAS, revealing that high-performing architectures cluster in flat regions while poor ones are isolated. The method introduces Architecture-Aware Minimization (A²M), a novel algorithmic framework that analytically biases gradient-based NAS towards flat minima in architecture space. Experimental results on NAS-Bench-201 and DARTS show that A²M consistently boosts test accuracy, achieving average improvements of +3.60% on CIFAR-10, +4.60% on CIFAR-100, and +3.64% on ImageNet16-120 over state-of-the-art methods.
本研究旨在探索神经架构搜索空间的几何特性以提升泛化能力，通过分析可微分NAS的损失景观，发现高性能架构聚集于平坦区域而次优架构孤立。方法上提出了架构感知最小化（A²M），这是一种新颖的算法框架，通过解析方式引导梯度搜索朝向架构空间的平坦最小值。在NAS-Bench-201和DARTS上的实验结果表明，A²M能持续提高测试精度，在CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100和ImageNet16-120数据集上平均分别提升3.60%、4.60%和3.64%，优于现有先进方法。
A Survey of Reinforcement Learning For Economics
Authors: Pranjal Rawat
First: 2026-03-09T21:43:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T15:45:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This survey (re)introduces reinforcement learning methods to economists. The curse of dimensionality limits how far exact dynamic programming can be effectively applied, forcing us to rely on suitably "small" problems or our ability to convert "big" problems into smaller ones. While this reduction has been sufficient for many classical applications, a growing class of economic models resists such reduction. Reinforcement learning algorithms offer a natural, sample-based extension of dynamic programming, extending tractability to problems with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. I review the theory connecting classical planning to modern learning algorithms and demonstrate their mechanics through simulated examples in pricing, inventory control, strategic games, and preference elicitation. I also examine the practical vulnerabilities of these algorithms, noting their brittleness, sample inefficiency, sensitivity to hyperparameters, and the absence of global convergence guarantees outside of tabular settings. The successes of reinforcement learning remain strictly bounded by these constraints, as well as a reliance on accurate simulators. When guided by economic structure, reinforcement learning provides a remarkably flexible framework. It stands as an imperfect, but promising, addition to the computational economist's toolkit. A companion survey (Rust and Rawat, 2026b) covers the inverse problem of inferring preferences from observed behavior. All simulation code is publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在经济学中的应用综述
本文向经济学家（重新）介绍了强化学习方法。维度灾难限制了精确动态规划的有效应用范围，迫使我们依赖适当的“小”问题或将“大”问题转化为较小问题的能力。尽管这种简化对许多经典应用已足够，但越来越多的经济模型难以进行此类简化。强化学习算法提供了一种基于样本的动态规划自然扩展，将可处理性延伸至高维状态、连续动作和策略交互的问题。本文回顾了连接经典规划与现代学习算法的理论，并通过定价、库存控制、策略博弈和偏好诱导的模拟示例展示其机制。同时，文章分析了这些算法的实际脆弱性，包括其脆弱性、样本效率低下、对超参数的敏感性，以及在非表格化场景中缺乏全局收敛保证。强化学习的成功仍严格受限于这些约束以及对精确模拟器的依赖。在经济结构的指导下，强化学习提供了一个极为灵活的框架，虽不完美但前景可期，是对计算经济学家工具箱的有力补充。配套综述（Rust与Rawat，2026b）涵盖了从观测行为推断偏好的逆问题。所有模拟代码均已公开。
Summary / 总结
This survey aims to introduce reinforcement learning (RL) to economists as a method to overcome the curse of dimensionality in dynamic programming, which limits classical approaches to small or reducible problems. The method involves using sample-based RL algorithms to extend tractability to economic models with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. Experimental results from simulated examples in pricing, inventory control, games, and preference elicitation demonstrate RL's flexibility, but also reveal practical vulnerabilities such as brittleness, sample inefficiency, hyperparameter sensitivity, and lack of global convergence guarantees, indicating its promise as an imperfect yet useful tool when guided by economic structure.
本综述旨在向经济学家介绍强化学习方法，以解决动态规划中维度灾难的限制，该限制迫使经典方法仅适用于小型或可简化的问题。该方法利用基于样本的强化学习算法，将可处理性扩展到具有高维状态、连续动作和策略互动的经济模型。在定价、库存控制、策略游戏和偏好引导的模拟实验结果表明，强化学习具有灵活性，但也揭示了其脆弱性、样本效率低下、超参数敏感性和缺乏全局收敛保证等实际弱点，表明在经济学结构指导下，它虽不完美但有望成为有用的工具。
A Learning Method with Gap-Aware Generation for Heterogeneous DAG Scheduling
Authors: Ruisong Zhou, Haijun Zou, Li Zhou, Chumin Sun, Zaiwen Wen
First: 2026-03-24T14:16:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T14:16:08+00:00
Comments: 30pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Efficient scheduling of directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) in heterogeneous environments is challenging due to resource capacities and dependencies. In practice, the need for adaptability across environments with varying resource pools and task types, alongside rapid schedule generation, complicates these challenges. We propose WeCAN, an end-to-end reinforcement learning framework for heterogeneous DAG scheduling that addresses task--pool compatibility coefficients and generation-induced optimality gaps. It adopts a two-stage single-pass design: a single forward pass produces task--pool scores and global parameters, followed by a generation map that constructs schedules without repeated network calls. Its weighted cross-attention encoder models task--pool interactions gated by compatibility coefficients, and is size-agnostic to environment fluctuations. Moreover, widely used list-scheduling maps can incur generation-induced optimality gaps from restricted reachability. We introduce an order-space analysis that characterizes the reachable set of generation maps via feasible schedule orders, explains the mechanism behind generation-induced gaps, and yields sufficient conditions for gap elimination. Guided by these conditions, we design a skip-extended realization with an analytically parameterized decreasing skip rule, which enlarges the reachable order set while preserving single-pass efficiency. Experiments on computation graphs and real-world TPC-H DAGs demonstrate improved makespan over strong baselines, with inference time comparable to classical heuristics and faster than multi-round neural schedulers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向异构DAG调度的间隙感知生成学习方法
在异构环境中，由于资源容量和任务依赖关系，有向无环图（DAG）的高效调度具有挑战性。实践中，跨资源池和任务类型多变的环境适应性需求以及快速生成调度的要求进一步加剧了复杂性。本文提出WeCAN，一种面向异构DAG调度的端到端强化学习框架，通过处理任务-资源池兼容性系数和生成过程引发的最优性间隙来解决该问题。该框架采用两阶段单次前向设计：单次前向传播生成任务-资源池评分与全局参数，随后通过生成映射无需重复网络调用即可构建调度方案。其加权交叉注意力编码器通过兼容性系数门控建模任务-资源池交互，且对环境规模波动具有无关性。此外，广泛使用的列表调度映射可能因可达性受限而产生生成性最优间隙。我们提出一种基于有序空间的分析方法，通过可行调度序列刻画生成映射的可达集合，阐释生成间隙的形成机制，并推导出消除间隙的充分条件。基于这些条件，我们设计了具有解析参数化递减跳跃规则的跳跃扩展实现方案，在保持单次前向效率的同时扩大可达序列集合。在计算图和实际TPC-H DAG上的实验表明，该方法在完工时间上优于强基线模型，推理时间与经典启发式算法相当，且快于多轮神经调度器。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of efficiently scheduling directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) in heterogeneous environments, where adaptability to varying resources and fast schedule generation are crucial. The authors propose WeCAN, an end-to-end reinforcement learning framework that uses a two-stage single-pass design: a forward pass computes task-pool scores and global parameters via a weighted cross-attention encoder, which models interactions gated by compatibility coefficients and is size-agnostic, followed by a generation map to construct schedules without repeated network calls. To mitigate generation-induced optimality gaps from restricted reachability in list-scheduling, they introduce an order-space analysis characterizing reachable schedule orders and design a skip-extended realization with a parameterized decreasing skip rule to enlarge the reachable set while maintaining efficiency. Experimental results on computation graphs and real-world TPC-H DAGs show improved makespan over strong baselines, with inference time comparable to classical heuristics and faster than multi-round neural schedulers.
本文针对异构环境中高效调度有向无环图（DAG）的挑战，其中需要适应不同资源并实现快速调度生成。作者提出了WeCAN，一种端到端的强化学习框架，采用两阶段单次设计：通过加权交叉注意力编码器进行前向传递，计算任务-资源池分数和全局参数，该编码器基于兼容性系数建模交互且尺寸无关，随后使用生成映射构建调度而无需重复网络调用。为缓解列表调度中因可达性受限导致的生成诱导最优性差距，他们引入了订单空间分析来表征可达调度订单，并设计了具有参数化递减跳过规则的跳过扩展实现，以扩大可达集同时保持效率。在计算图和真实TPC-H DAG上的实验结果表明，相比强基线方法，该方法缩短了完工时间，且推理时间与经典启发式算法相当，快于多轮神经调度器。
Neural ODE and SDE Models for Adaptation and Planning in Model-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chao Han, Stefanos Ioannou, Luca Manneschi, T. J. Hayward, Michael Mangan, Aditya Gilra, Eleni Vasilaki
Venue: Transactions on Machine Learning Research (10/2025)
First: 2026-03-24T14:12:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T14:12:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We investigate neural ordinary and stochastic differential equations (neural ODEs and SDEs) to model stochastic dynamics in fully and partially observed environments within a model-based reinforcement learning (RL) framework. Through a sequence of simulations, we show that neural SDEs more effectively capture the inherent stochasticity of transition dynamics, enabling high-performing policies with improved sample efficiency in challenging scenarios. We leverage neural ODEs and SDEs for efficient policy adaptation to changes in environment dynamics via inverse models, requiring only limited interactions with the new environment. To address partial observability, we introduce a latent SDE model that combines an ODE with a GAN-trained stochastic component in latent space. Policies derived from this model provide a strong baseline, outperforming or matching general model-based and model-free approaches across stochastic continuous-control benchmarks. This work demonstrates the applicability of action-conditional latent SDEs for RL planning in environments with stochastic transitions. Our code is available at: https://github.com/ChaoHan-UoS/NeuralRL
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于神经ODE与SDE的模型强化学习中的适应与规划方法
本研究在基于模型的强化学习框架下，探索利用神经常微分方程与随机微分方程（神经ODE与SDE）对完全可观测及部分可观测环境中的随机动力学进行建模。通过系列仿真实验，我们证明神经SDE能更有效地捕捉状态转移的内在随机性，在复杂场景中实现更高性能的策略并提升样本效率。我们借助逆模型，通过神经ODE与SDE实现策略对环境动态变化的高效适应，仅需与新环境进行有限交互。针对部分可观测问题，我们提出一种潜在空间SDE模型，将ODE与GAN训练的随机分量相结合。基于该模型推导的策略形成了强基准线，在随机连续控制基准测试中超越或匹配主流基于模型及无模型方法。本工作验证了动作条件潜在SDE在随机转移环境强化学习规划中的适用性。代码已开源：https://github.com/ChaoHan-UoS/NeuralRL
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to model stochastic dynamics in model-based reinforcement learning (RL) for both fully and partially observed environments. The method employs neural ordinary and stochastic differential equations (neural ODEs and SDEs), introducing a latent SDE model that combines an ODE with a GAN-trained stochastic component to handle partial observability. The main experimental results show that neural SDEs more effectively capture transition stochasticity, leading to high-performing policies with improved sample efficiency, and the proposed model provides a strong baseline that matches or outperforms general model-based and model-free approaches on stochastic continuous-control benchmarks, while also enabling efficient policy adaptation to new dynamics via inverse models.
本文的研究动机是基于模型的强化学习需要为完全和部分可观测环境中的随机动力学进行建模。方法上采用了神经常微分方程和随机微分方程，并引入了一个潜在随机微分方程模型，该模型结合了常微分方程与一个由GAN训练的随机组件来处理部分可观测性。主要实验结果表明，神经随机微分方程能更有效地捕捉转移随机性，从而产生具有更高样本效率的高性能策略；所提出的模型提供了一个强大的基线，在随机连续控制基准测试中匹配或超越了通用的基于模型和无模型方法，同时还能通过逆模型实现对新动力学的高效策略适应。
GEM: Guided Expectation-Maximization for Behavior-Normalized Candidate Action Selection in Offline RL
Authors: Haoyu Wang, Jingcheng Wang, Shunyu Wu, Xinwei Xiao
First: 2026-03-24T14:04:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T14:04:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning (RL) can fit strong value functions from fixed datasets, yet reliable deployment still hinges on the action selection interface used to query them. When the dataset induces a branched or multimodal action landscape, unimodal policy extraction can blur competing hypotheses and yield "in-between" actions that are weakly supported by data, making decisions brittle even with a strong critic. We introduce GEM (Guided Expectation-Maximization), an analytical framework that makes action selection both multimodal and explicitly controllable. GEM trains a Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM) actor via critic-guided, advantage-weighted EM-style updates that preserve distinct components while shifting probability mass toward high-value regions, and learns a tractable GMM behavior model to quantify support. During inference, GEM performs candidate-based selection: it generates a parallel candidate set and reranks actions using a conservative ensemble lower-confidence bound together with behavior-normalized support, where the behavior log-likelihood is standardized within each state's candidate set to yield stable, comparable control across states and candidate budgets. Empirically, GEM is competitive across D4RL benchmarks, and offers a simple inference-time budget knob (candidate count) that trades compute for decision quality without retraining.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GEM：离线强化学习中基于行为归一化候选动作选择的引导期望最大化算法
离线强化学习（RL）能够从固定数据集中拟合出强大的价值函数，但其可靠部署仍取决于用于查询这些函数的动作选择接口。当数据集诱导出分支或多模态动作空间时，单模态策略提取会模糊竞争假设，并产生数据支持较弱的“中间”动作，导致即使具有强大评判器时决策仍显脆弱。本文提出GEM（引导期望最大化）——一种使动作选择兼具多模态性与显式可控性的分析框架。GEM通过评判器引导、优势加权的EM式更新训练高斯混合模型（GMM）执行器，在保持不同分量的同时将概率质量向高价值区域转移，并学习可处理的GMM行为模型以量化支持度。在推理阶段，GEM执行基于候选集的选择：生成并行候选集，并采用保守集成下界置信度与行为归一化支持度对动作进行重排序，其中行为对数似然在每个状态的候选集内标准化，以实现跨状态和候选预算的稳定可比控制。实验表明，GEM在D4RL基准测试中具有竞争力，并提供简单的推理时预算调节旋钮（候选数量），可在无需重新训练的情况下以计算量换取决策质量。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge in offline reinforcement learning where unimodal policy extraction from multimodal datasets can produce unsupported 'in-between' actions, leading to brittle decisions despite strong value functions. The method introduces GEM (Guided Expectation-Maximization), which trains a Gaussian Mixture Model actor using critic-guided, advantage-weighted updates to maintain distinct action modes while shifting probability toward high-value regions, and learns a behavior model to quantify data support; during inference, it generates parallel action candidates and reranks them using a conservative ensemble bound and behavior-normalized support, with a candidate count knob to trade compute for quality. Experimental results show GEM is competitive on D4RL benchmarks, offering stable control and improved decision quality through its adjustable inference budget.
本文的动机源于离线强化学习中，从多模态数据集中提取单模态策略可能产生缺乏数据支持的'中间'动作，导致决策脆弱，即使价值函数很强。方法上提出了GEM（引导期望最大化），它通过批评者引导、优势加权的更新训练高斯混合模型行动者，以保持不同的动作模式同时将概率向高价值区域转移，并学习行为模型来量化数据支持；在推理时，它生成并行动作候选集，并使用保守集成下界和行为归一化支持进行重排序，通过候选数量调节计算与质量的权衡。实验结果表明，GEM在D4RL基准测试中具有竞争力，通过可调整的推理预算提供了稳定的控制和改进的决策质量。
ImplicitRM: Unbiased Reward Modeling from Implicit Preference Data for LLM alignment
Authors: Hao Wang, Haocheng Yang, Licheng Pan, Lei Shen, Xiaoxi Li, Yinuo Wang, Zhichao Chen, Yuan Lu, Haoxuan Li, Zhouchen Lin
First: 2026-03-24T13:32:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T13:32:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward modeling represents a long-standing challenge in reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) for aligning language models. Current reward modeling is heavily contingent upon experimental feedback data with high collection costs. In this work, we study \textit{implicit reward modeling} -- learning reward models from implicit human feedback (e.g., clicks and copies) -- as a cost-effective alternative. We identify two fundamental challenges in implicit reward modeling: (1) Implicit preference data lacks definitive negative samples, which makes standard positive-negative classification methods inapplicable; (2) Implicit preference data suffers from user preference bias, where different responses have different propensities to elicit user feedback actions, which exacerbates the difficulty of distinguishing definitive negative samples. To address these challenges, we propose ImplicitRM, which aims to learn unbiased reward models from implicit preference data. ImplicitRM stratifies training samples into four latent groups via a stratification model. Building on this, it derives a learning objective through likelihood maximization, which we prove is theoretically unbiased, effectively resolving both challenges. Experiments demonstrate that ImplicitRM learns accurate reward models across implicit preference datasets. Code is available on our project website.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ImplicitRM：从隐式偏好数据中无偏奖励建模用于大语言模型对齐
奖励建模是基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）中对齐语言模型的一项长期挑战。当前奖励建模高度依赖收集成本高昂的实验反馈数据。本研究探讨了隐式奖励建模——从隐式人类反馈（如点击、复制）中学习奖励模型——作为一种经济高效的替代方案。我们识别出隐式奖励建模的两个根本挑战：（1）隐式偏好数据缺乏明确的负样本，导致标准的正负分类方法失效；（2）隐式偏好数据存在用户偏好偏差，即不同回复引发用户反馈行为的倾向性不同，这加剧了区分明确负样本的难度。为解决这些挑战，我们提出ImplicitRM，旨在从隐式偏好数据中学习无偏奖励模型。该方法通过分层模型将训练样本划分为四个潜在组别，并基于此通过似然最大化推导出学习目标。我们证明该目标在理论上具有无偏性，能有效解决上述两个挑战。实验表明，ImplicitRM能在多种隐式偏好数据集上学习到准确的奖励模型。代码已在项目网站公开。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the high cost of collecting explicit human feedback for reward modeling in language model alignment by proposing ImplicitRM, a method to learn unbiased reward models from implicit feedback like clicks and copies. The motivation stems from two challenges: implicit data lacks definitive negative samples and suffers from user preference bias, making standard classification methods inapplicable. The method involves stratifying training samples into four latent groups via a stratification model and deriving a theoretically unbiased learning objective through likelihood maximization. Experimental results show that ImplicitRM successfully learns accurate reward models across various implicit preference datasets, validating its effectiveness as a cost-effective alternative.
本文针对语言模型对齐中显式人类反馈收集成本高的问题，提出了ImplicitRM方法，旨在从点击、复制等隐式反馈中学习无偏的奖励模型。其动机源于隐式数据缺乏明确的负样本且存在用户偏好偏差，这使得标准的正负分类方法不适用。该方法通过分层模型将训练样本分为四个潜在组，并基于似然最大化推导出理论上无偏的学习目标，有效解决了上述挑战。实验结果表明，ImplicitRM能够在多种隐式偏好数据集上学习到准确的奖励模型，验证了其作为成本效益替代方案的有效性。
MorphoNAS: Embryogenic Neural Architecture Search Through Morphogen-Guided Development
Authors: Mykola Glybovets, Sergii Medvid
Venue: Kibernetyka i Systemnyj Analiz, 62(2), 2026
First: 2025-07-18T09:57:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T12:30:09+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 8 figures. Published in Kibernetyka i Systemnyj Analiz (Cybernetics and Systems Analysis), vol. 62, no. 2, 2026. English translation by Springer Nature forthcoming. v2: Aligned with published version; corrected author email address
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While biological neural networks develop from compact genomes using relatively simple rules, modern artificial neural architecture search methods mostly involve explicit and routine manual work. In this paper, we introduce MorphoNAS (Morphogenetic Neural Architecture Search), a system able to deterministically grow neural networks through morphogenetic self-organization inspired by the Free Energy Principle, reaction-diffusion systems, and gene regulatory networks. In MorphoNAS, simple genomes encode just morphogens dynamics and threshold-based rules of cellular development. Nevertheless, this leads to self-organization of a single progenitor cell into complex neural networks, while the entire process is built on local chemical interactions. Our evolutionary experiments focused on two different domains: structural targeting, in which MorphoNAS system was able to find fully successful genomes able to generate predefined random graph configurations (8-31 nodes); and functional performance on the CartPole control task achieving low complexity 6-7 neuron solutions when target network size minimization evolutionary pressure was applied. The evolutionary process successfully balanced between quality of of the final solutions and neural architecture search effectiveness. Overall, our findings suggest that the proposed MorphoNAS method is able to grow complex specific neural architectures, using simple developmental rules, which suggests a feasible biological route to adaptive and efficient neural architecture search.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MorphoNAS：基于形态发生素引导发育的胚胎式神经架构搜索
生物神经网络通过相对简单的规则从紧凑基因组发育而成，而现代人工神经架构搜索方法大多依赖显式且常规的手动操作。本文提出MorphoNAS（形态发生神经架构搜索）系统，该系统受自由能原理、反应-扩散系统和基因调控网络启发，通过形态发生自组织实现神经网络的确定性生长。在MorphoNAS中，简单基因组仅编码形态发生素动力学和基于阈值的细胞发育规则，却能驱动单个祖细胞通过局部化学相互作用自组织成复杂神经网络。进化实验聚焦两个领域：在结构定向任务中，系统成功找到能生成预定随机图配置（8-31节点）的基因组；在CartPole控制任务中，施加网络规模最小化进化压力后获得仅需6-7个神经元的高效解。进化过程在解决方案质量与架构搜索效率间取得平衡。研究表明，MorphoNAS能通过简单发育规则生长出复杂特化神经架构，为自适应高效神经架构搜索提供了可行的生物学路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the contrast between the compact, self-organizing development of biological neural networks and the manual, explicit nature of conventional neural architecture search, this paper introduces MorphoNAS, a method that deterministically grows neural networks through morphogenetic self-organization inspired by biological principles like the Free Energy Principle and reaction-diffusion systems. The method employs simple genomes encoding only morphogen dynamics and threshold-based cellular development rules, enabling a single progenitor cell to self-organize into complex architectures via local chemical interactions. Experimental results demonstrate the system's capability in structural targeting, successfully generating predefined random graph configurations of 8-31 nodes, and in functional performance on the CartPole control task, where it evolved low-complexity solutions of 6-7 neurons under size minimization pressure, effectively balancing solution quality and search efficiency.
本文的动机源于生物神经网络紧凑、自组织的发展方式与传统神经架构搜索手动、显式特性之间的对比，提出了MorphoNAS方法，该方法通过受自由能原理和反应-扩散系统等生物学原理启发的形态发生自组织，确定性生长神经网络。该方法使用仅编码形态发生素动力学和基于阈值的细胞发育规则的简单基因组，使得单个祖细胞能通过局部化学相互作用自组织成复杂架构。实验结果表明，该系统在结构目标上能成功生成8-31个节点的预定义随机图配置，在CartPole控制任务的功能性能上，在尺寸最小化压力下演化出6-7个神经元的低复杂度解决方案，有效平衡了解决方案质量与搜索效率。
SpecXMaster Technical Report
Authors: Yutang Ge, Yaning Cui, Hanzheng Li, Jun-Jie Wang, Fanjie Xu, Jinhan Dong, Yongqi Jin, Dongxu Cui, Peng Jin, Guojiang Zhao, Hengxing Cai, Rong Zhu, Linfeng Zhang, Xiaohong Ji, Zhifeng Gao
First: 2026-03-24T11:49:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T11:49:41+00:00
Comments: Technical report from DP Technology.21 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Intelligent spectroscopy serves as a pivotal element in AI-driven closed-loop scientific discovery, functioning as the critical bridge between matter structure and artificial intelligence. However, conventional expert-dependent spectral interpretation encounters substantial hurdles, including susceptibility to human bias and error, dependence on limited specialized expertise, and variability across interpreters. To address these challenges, we propose SpecXMaster, an intelligent framework leveraging Agentic Reinforcement Learning (RL) for NMR molecular spectral interpretation. SpecXMaster enables automated extraction of multiplicity information from both 1H and 13C spectra directly from raw FID (free induction decay) data. This end-to-end pipeline enables fully automated interpretation of NMR spectra into chemical structures. It demonstrates superior performance across multiple public NMR interpretation benchmarks and has been refined through iterative evaluations by professional chemical spectroscopists. We believe that SpecXMaster, as a novel methodological paradigm for spectral interpretation, will have a profound impact on the organic chemistry community.

Policy-based Tuning of Autoregressive Image Models with Instance- and Distribution-Level Rewards
Authors: Orhun Buğra Baran, Melih Kandemir, Ramazan Gokberk Cinbis
First: 2026-03-24T11:28:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T11:28:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autoregressive (AR) models are highly effective for image generation, yet their standard maximum-likelihood estimation training lacks direct optimization for sample quality and diversity. While reinforcement learning (RL) has been used to align diffusion models, these methods typically suffer from output diversity collapse. Similarly, concurrent RL methods for AR models rely strictly on instance-level rewards, often trading off distributional coverage for quality. To address these limitations, we propose a lightweight RL framework that casts token-based AR synthesis as a Markov Decision Process, optimized via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Our core contribution is the introduction of a novel distribution-level Leave-One-Out FID (LOO-FID) reward; by leveraging an exponential moving average of feature moments, it explicitly encourages sample diversity and prevents mode collapse during policy updates. We integrate this with composite instance-level rewards (CLIP and HPSv2) for strict semantic and perceptual fidelity, and stabilize the multi-objective learning with an adaptive entropy regularization term. Extensive experiments on LlamaGen and VQGAN architectures demonstrate clear improvements across standard quality and diversity metrics within only a few hundred tuning iterations. The results also show that the model can be updated to produce competitive samples even without Classifier-Free Guidance, and bypass its 2x inference cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于策略的自回归图像模型调优：结合实例级与分布级奖励
自回归模型在图像生成中表现卓越，但其标准的最大似然估计训练缺乏对样本质量和多样性的直接优化。虽然强化学习已被用于对齐扩散模型，但这些方法常面临输出多样性崩溃的问题。类似地，当前针对自回归模型的强化学习方法严格依赖实例级奖励，往往以牺牲分布覆盖度为代价换取质量提升。为突破这些局限，我们提出一种轻量级强化学习框架，将基于令牌的自回归合成建模为马尔可夫决策过程，并通过组相对策略优化进行优化。我们的核心贡献是引入了一种新颖的分布级留一FID奖励：通过利用特征矩的指数移动平均，该奖励显式促进样本多样性，并在策略更新过程中防止模式崩溃。我们将其与复合实例级奖励相结合，以确保严格的语义和感知保真度，并通过自适应熵正则化项稳定多目标学习。在LlamaGen和VQGAN架构上的大量实验表明，仅需数百次调优迭代，模型在标准质量与多样性指标上均获得显著提升。结果还显示，即使不使用无分类器引导，模型仍可通过更新生成具有竞争力的样本，从而规避其两倍的推理成本。

To overcome this, the authors propose a lightweight RL framework that treats token-based autoregressive synthesis as a Markov Decision Process, optimized via Group Relative Policy Optimization, and introduce a novel distribution-level Leave-One-Out FID reward to explicitly encourage diversity and prevent mode collapse, combined with instance-level rewards for semantic and perceptual fidelity. MedCausalX: Adaptive Causal Reasoning with Self-Reflection for Trustworthy Medical Vision-Language Models
Authors: Jianxin Lin, Chunzheng Zhu, Peter J. Kneuertz, Yunfei Bai, Yuan Xue
First: 2026-03-24T11:28:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T11:28:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have enabled interpretable medical diagnosis by integrating visual perception with linguistic reasoning. Yet, existing medical chain-of-thought (CoT) models lack explicit mechanisms to represent and enforce causal reasoning, leaving them vulnerable to spurious correlations and limiting their clinical reliability. We pinpoint three core challenges in medical CoT reasoning: how to adaptively trigger causal correction, construct high-quality causal-spurious contrastive samples, and maintain causal consistency across reasoning trajectories. To address these challenges, we propose MedCausalX, an end-to-end framework explicitly models causal reasoning chains in medical VLMs. We first introduce the CRMed dataset providing fine-grained anatomical annotations, structured causal reasoning chains, and counterfactual variants that guide the learning of causal relationships beyond superficial correlations. Building upon CRMed, MedCausalX employs a two-stage adaptive reflection architecture equipped with $\langle$causal$\rangle$ and $\langle$verify$\rangle$ tokens, enabling the model to autonomously determine when and how to perform causal analysis and verification. Finally, a trajectory-level causal correction objective optimized through error-attributed reinforcement learning refines the reasoning chain, allowing the model to distinguish genuine causal dependencies from shortcut associations. Extensive experiments on multiple benchmarks show that MedCausalX consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, improving diagnostic consistency by +5.4 points, reducing hallucination by over 10 points, and attaining top spatial grounding IoU, thereby setting a new standard for causally grounded medical reasoning.

Information Gain-based Policy Optimization: A Simple and Effective Approach for Multi-Turn Search Agents
Authors: Guoqing Wang, Sunhao Dai, Guangze Ye, Zeyu Gan, Wei Yao, Yong Deng, Xiaofeng Wu, Zhenzhe Ying
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-16T17:59:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T11:14:54+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model (LLM)-based agents are increasingly trained with reinforcement learning (RL) to enhance their ability to interact with external environments through tool use, particularly in search-based settings that require multi-turn reasoning and knowledge acquisition. However, existing approaches typically rely on outcome-based rewards that are only provided exclusively upon generating the final answer. This reward sparsity becomes particularly problematic in multi-turn settings, where long trajectories exacerbate three critical issues: (i) advantage collapse, where all rollouts receive identical rewards and provide no useful learning signals; (ii) lack of fine-grained credit assignment, where the correctness of intermediate turns is obscured, especially in long-horizon tasks; and (iii) poor sample efficiency, where each rollout yields only a single outcome signal, leading to low data utilization. In this paper, we propose Information Gain-based Policy Optimization (IGPO), a simple yet effective RL framework that provides dense and intrinsic supervision for multi-turn agent training. IGPO models each interaction turn as an incremental process of acquiring information about the ground truth, and defines turn-level rewards as the marginal increase in the policy's probability of producing the correct answer. Unlike prior process-level reward approaches that depend on external reward models or costly Monte Carlo estimation, IGPO derives intrinsic rewards directly from the model's own belief updates. These intrinsic turn-level rewards are combined with outcome-level supervision to form dense reward signals. Extensive experiments on both in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks demonstrate that IGPO consistently outperforms strong baselines in multi-turn scenarios, achieving higher accuracy and improved data efficiency. Our code is available at https://github.com/GuoqingWang1/IGPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于信息增益的策略优化：一种面向多轮搜索智能体的简洁高效方法
基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体越来越多地通过强化学习（RL）进行训练，以增强其通过工具使用与外部环境交互的能力，尤其是在需要多轮推理和知识获取的搜索场景中。然而，现有方法通常依赖于基于结果的奖励，仅在生成最终答案时提供。这种奖励稀疏性在多轮场景中尤为突出，长轨迹会加剧三个关键问题：（i）优势崩溃，所有推演获得相同奖励且无法提供有效学习信号；（ii）缺乏细粒度信用分配，中间轮次的正确性被掩盖，尤其在长周期任务中；（iii）样本效率低下，每次推演仅产生单一结果信号，导致数据利用率低。本文提出基于信息增益的策略优化（IGPO），这是一种简洁而有效的RL框架，为多轮智能体训练提供密集的内在监督。IGPO将每次交互轮次建模为获取真实信息增量过程，并将轮次级奖励定义为策略生成正确答案概率的边际增长。与依赖外部奖励模型或昂贵蒙特卡洛估计的现有过程级奖励方法不同，IGPO直接从模型自身的信念更新中推导内在奖励。这些内在轮次级奖励与结果级监督相结合，形成密集奖励信号。在领域内和领域外基准上的大量实验表明，IGPO在多轮场景中持续优于强基线方法，实现了更高准确率和更优数据效率。代码发布于 https://github.com/GuoqingWang1/IGPO。

To overcome this, the authors propose Information Gain-based Policy Optimization (IGPO), a reinforcement learning framework that provides dense supervision by modeling each interaction turn as an incremental information acquisition process and defining turn-level rewards as the marginal increase in the policy's probability of producing the correct answer, derived intrinsically from the model's own belief updates. Experimental results on in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks show that IGPO consistently outperforms strong baselines, achieving higher accuracy and improved data efficiency in multi-turn scenarios.
本文针对基于大语言模型的多轮搜索智能体训练中仅依赖最终结果的稀疏奖励所导致的优势崩溃、细粒度信用分配困难及样本效率低下等问题，提出了一种信息增益策略优化方法。该方法通过将每次交互建模为逐步获取信息的过程，并基于模型自身信念更新的边际概率增加来定义轮次级内在奖励，从而提供密集的监督信号。在领域内和领域外基准测试上的广泛实验表明，该方法在多轮场景中持续优于现有基线，实现了更高的准确性和数据效率。
DeepXplain: XAI-Guided Autonomous Defense Against Multi-Stage APT Campaigns
Authors: Trung V. Phan, Thomas Bauschert
First: 2026-03-22T15:36:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T10:02:49+00:00
Comments: This paper is currently under review for IEEE GLOBECOM 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Advanced Persistent Threats (APTs) are stealthy, multi-stage attacks that require adaptive and timely defense. While deep reinforcement learning (DRL) enables autonomous cyber defense, its decisions are often opaque and difficult to trust in operational environments. This paper presents DeepXplain, an explainable DRL framework for stage-aware APT defense. Building on our prior DeepStage model, DeepXplain integrates provenance-based graph learning, temporal stage estimation, and a unified XAI pipeline that provides structural, temporal, and policy-level explanations. Unlike post-hoc methods, explanation signals are incorporated directly into policy optimization through evidence alignment and confidence-aware reward shaping. To the best of our knowledge, DeepXplain is the first framework to integrate explanation signals into reinforcement learning for APT defense. Experiments in a realistic enterprise testbed show improvements in stage-weighted F1-score (0.887 to 0.915) and success rate (84.7% to 89.6%), along with higher explanation confidence (0.86), improved fidelity (0.79), and more compact explanations (0.31). These results demonstrate enhanced effectiveness and trustworthiness of autonomous cyber defense.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeepXplain：面向多阶段APT攻击的XAI引导自主防御框架
高级持续性威胁（APT）是隐蔽的多阶段攻击，需要自适应且及时的防御。虽然深度强化学习（DRL）能够实现自主网络防御，但其决策在操作环境中往往不透明且难以信任。本文提出DeepXplain——一种面向阶段感知型APT防御的可解释DRL框架。该框架基于我们先前提出的DeepStage模型，整合了基于溯源关系的图学习、时序阶段估计，以及提供结构、时序与策略级解释的统一可解释人工智能（XAI）流水线。与事后解释方法不同，DeepXplain通过证据对齐和置信度感知的奖励塑造机制，将解释信号直接融入策略优化过程。据我们所知，这是首个将解释信号集成至强化学习中以实现APT防御的框架。在真实企业测试环境中的实验表明：该框架将阶段加权F1分数从0.887提升至0.915，成功率从84.7%提升至89.6%，同时获得更高的解释置信度（0.86）、改进的保真度（0.79）以及更紧凑的解释（0.31）。这些结果证明了自主网络防御在效能与可信度方面的双重提升。

Experimental results in a realistic enterprise testbed demonstrate improvements in stage-weighted F1-score (from 0.887 to 0.915) and success rate (from 84.7% to 89.6%), alongside higher explanation confidence (0.86), improved fidelity (0.79), and more compact explanations (0.31), thereby enhancing both the effectiveness and trustworthiness of the defense system.
本文针对隐蔽、多阶段的先进持续性威胁（APT）需要可信的自主防御问题，提出了DeepXplain这一可解释的深度强化学习（DRL）框架。其动机源于标准DRL在操作化网络防御中决策的不透明性。该方法将基于溯源数据的图学习和时序阶段估计与一个统一的可解释人工智能（XAI）流程相结合，提供结构、时序和策略层面的解释；关键创新在于，解释信号通过证据对齐和置信度感知的奖励塑造直接融入策略优化，而非事后应用。在真实企业测试环境中的实验结果表明，该框架在阶段加权F1分数（从0.887提升至0.915）和成功率（从84.7%提升至89.6%）上均有改善，同时获得了更高的解释置信度（0.86）、改进的保真度（0.79）以及更简洁的解释（0.31），从而提升了防御系统的有效性和可信度。
RedTopic: Toward Topic-Diverse Red Teaming of Large Language Models
Authors: Jiale Ding, Xiang Zheng, Yutao Wu, Cong Wang, Wei-Bin Lee, Ling Pan, Xingjun Ma, Yu-Gang Jiang
First: 2025-06-17T10:55:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T09:55:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as black-box components in real-world applications, red teaming has become essential for identifying potential risks. It tests LLMs with adversarial prompts to uncover vulnerabilities and improve safety alignment. Ideally, effective red teaming should be adaptive to evolving LLM capabilities and explore a broad range of harmful topics. However, existing approaches face two limitations: 1) topic-based approaches rely on pre-collected harmful topics, limited in flexibility and adaptivity. 2) topic-free methods use reinforcement learning (RL), but they lack an explicit reward signal for exploration and tend to over-optimize a narrow objective, reducing topic diversity. To address these limitations, we propose RedTopic, a novel red teaming framework that generates topic-diverse adversarial prompts through a contextualized generation pipeline, an aggregate reward design, and a multi-objective RL training loop. Experiments show that RedTopic produces more effective and diverse adversarial prompts than existing methods, with notable improvements in integrated evaluation metrics. We believe RedTopic represents a step toward more adaptive and topic-diverse red teaming for large language models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RedTopic：面向大语言模型的主题多样化红队测试

Learning The Minimum Action Distance
Authors: Lorenzo Steccanella, Joshua B. Evans, Özgür Şimşek, Anders Jonsson
First: 2025-06-10T22:27:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T09:31:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper presents a state representation framework for Markov decision processes (MDPs) that can be learned solely from state trajectories, requiring neither reward signals nor the actions executed by the agent. We propose learning the minimum action distance (MAD), defined as the minimum number of actions required to transition between states, as a fundamental metric that captures the underlying structure of an environment. MAD naturally enables critical downstream tasks such as goal-conditioned reinforcement learning and reward shaping by providing a dense, geometrically meaningful measure of progress. Our self-supervised learning approach constructs an embedding space where the distances between embedded state pairs correspond to their MAD, accommodating both symmetric and asymmetric approximations. We evaluate the framework on a comprehensive suite of environments with known MAD values, encompassing both deterministic and stochastic dynamics, as well as discrete and continuous state spaces, and environments with noisy observations. Empirical results demonstrate that the proposed approach not only efficiently learns accurate MAD representations across these diverse settings but also significantly outperforms existing state representation methods in terms of representation quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习最小动作距离
本文提出了一种用于马尔可夫决策过程的状态表示框架，该框架仅从状态轨迹中学习，无需奖励信号或智能体执行的动作。我们提出学习最小动作距离，定义为状态间转换所需的最小动作数，作为捕捉环境底层结构的基本度量。MAD通过提供密集且几何意义明确的进度度量，自然支持目标条件强化学习和奖励塑形等关键下游任务。我们的自监督学习方法构建了一个嵌入空间，其中嵌入状态对之间的距离对应其MAD，兼容对称和非对称近似。我们在已知MAD值的综合环境套件上评估该框架，涵盖确定性和随机动态、离散和连续状态空间，以及含噪声观测的环境。实证结果表明，所提方法不仅能在这些多样化设置中高效学习准确的MAD表示，而且在表示质量上显著优于现有状态表示方法。

Motivated by the need for state representations that capture intrinsic environment structure without relying on rewards or action labels, this paper introduces the Minimum Action Distance (MAD) as a fundamental metric, defined as the minimum number of actions needed to transition between states. The method employs a self-supervised learning framework to construct an embedding space where distances between state pairs approximate their MAD, handling both symmetric and asymmetric cases. Experimental results across diverse environments, including deterministic, stochastic, discrete, continuous, and noisy settings, demonstrate that the approach efficiently learns accurate MAD representations and outperforms existing state representation methods in quality.

Weak-PDE-Net: Discovering Open-Form PDEs via Differentiable Symbolic Networks and Weak Formulation
Authors: Xinxin Li, Xingyu Cui, Jin Qi, Juan Zhang, Da Li, Junping Yin
First: 2026-03-24T08:47:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T08:47:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Discovering governing Partial Differential Equations (PDEs) from sparse and noisy data is a challenging issue in data-driven scientific computing. Conventional sparse regression methods often suffer from two major limitations: (i) the instability of numerical differentiation under sparse and noisy data, and (ii) the restricted flexibility of a pre-defined candidate library. We propose Weak-PDE-Net, an end-to-end differentiable framework that can robustly identify open-form PDEs. Weak-PDE-Net consists of two interconnected modules: a forward response learner and a weak-form PDE generator. The learner embeds learnable Gaussian kernels within a lightweight MLP, serving as a surrogate model that adaptively captures system dynamics from sparse observations. Meanwhile, the generator integrates a symbolic network with an integral module to construct weak-form PDEs, avoiding explicit numerical differentiation and improving robustness to noise. To relax the constraints of the pre-defined library, we leverage Differentiable Neural Architecture Search strategy during training to explore the functional space, which enables the efficient discovery of open-form PDEs. The capability of Weak-PDE-Net in multivariable systems discovery is further enhanced by incorporating Galilean Invariance constraints and symmetry equivariance hypotheses to ensure physical consistency. Experiments on several challenging PDE benchmarks demonstrate that Weak-PDE-Net accurately recovers governing equations, even under highly sparse and noisy observations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Weak-PDE-Net：基于可微符号网络与弱形式求解发现开形式偏微分方程
从稀疏噪声数据中发现控制偏微分方程是数据驱动科学计算中的难题。传统稀疏回归方法常受两大限制：(i) 稀疏噪声数据下数值微分的不稳定性，(ii) 预定义候选函数库的灵活性受限。本文提出Weak-PDE-Net——一种能稳健识别开形式PDE的端到端可微框架。该框架包含两个互联模块：前向响应学习器与弱形式PDE生成器。学习器在轻量级MLP中嵌入可学习高斯核，作为自适应捕捉稀疏观测系统动态的代理模型；生成器则集成符号网络与积分模块构建弱形式PDE，避免显式数值微分并提升噪声鲁棒性。为突破预定义库约束，训练中采用可微神经架构搜索策略探索函数空间，实现开形式PDE的高效发现。通过引入伽利略不变性约束与对称等变性假设确保物理一致性，进一步增强了多变量系统发现能力。在多个挑战性PDE基准测试中，Weak-PDE-Net即使在高度稀疏噪声观测下仍能准确还原控制方程。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of discovering governing Partial Differential Equations (PDEs) from sparse and noisy data, where traditional sparse regression methods are limited by instability in numerical differentiation and inflexible pre-defined candidate libraries. The proposed Weak-PDE-Net is an end-to-end differentiable framework that combines a forward response learner using learnable Gaussian kernels in a lightweight MLP to model system dynamics, and a weak-form PDE generator integrating a symbolic network with an integral module to avoid explicit differentiation and enhance noise robustness. It employs Differentiable Neural Architecture Search to explore functional spaces for open-form PDE discovery and incorporates Galilean Invariance and symmetry equivariance for physical consistency in multivariable systems. Experimental results on PDE benchmarks show that Weak-PDE-Net accurately recovers equations even under highly sparse and noisy conditions.

CellFluxRL: Biologically-Constrained Virtual Cell Modeling via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dongxia Wu, Shiye Su, Yuhui Zhang, Elaine Sui, Emma Lundberg, Emily B. Fox, Serena Yeung-Levy
First: 2026-03-23T09:33:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T08:41:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Building virtual cells with generative models to simulate cellular behavior in silico is emerging as a promising paradigm for accelerating drug discovery. However, prior image-based generative approaches can produce implausible cell images that violate basic physical and biological constraints. To address this, we propose to post-train virtual cell models with reinforcement learning (RL), leveraging biologically meaningful evaluators as reward functions. We design seven rewards spanning three categories-biological function, structural validity, and morphological correctness-and optimize the state-of-the-art CellFlux model to yield CellFluxRL. CellFluxRL consistently improves over CellFlux across all rewards, with further performance boosts from test-time scaling. Overall, our results present a virtual cell modeling framework that enforces physically-based constraints through RL, advancing beyond "visually realistic" generations towards "biologically meaningful" ones.

EVA: Efficient Reinforcement Learning for End-to-End Video Agent
Authors: Yaolun Zhang, Ruohui Wang, Jiahao Wang, Yepeng Tang, Xuanyu Zheng, Haonan Duan, Hao Lu, Hanming Deng, Lewei Lu
First: 2026-03-24T08:06:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T08:06:29+00:00
Comments: CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Video understanding with multimodal large language models (MLLMs) remains challenging due to the long token sequences of videos, which contain extensive temporal dependencies and redundant frames. Existing approaches typically treat MLLMs as passive recognizers, processing entire videos or uniformly sampled frames without adaptive reasoning. Recent agent-based methods introduce external tools, yet still depend on manually designed workflows and perception-first strategies, resulting in inefficiency on long videos. We present EVA, an Efficient Reinforcement Learning framework for End-to-End Video Agent, which enables planning-before-perception through iterative summary-plan-action-reflection reasoning. EVA autonomously decides what to watch, when to watch, and how to watch, achieving query-driven and efficient video understanding. To train such agents, we design a simple yet effective three-stage learning pipeline - comprising supervised fine-tuning (SFT), Kahneman-Tversky Optimization (KTO), and Generalized Reward Policy Optimization (GRPO) - that bridges supervised imitation and reinforcement learning. We further construct high-quality datasets for each stage, supporting stable and reproducible training. We evaluate EVA on six video understanding benchmarks, demonstrating its comprehensive capabilities. Compared with existing baselines, EVA achieves a substantial improvement of 6-12% over general MLLM baselines and a further 1-3% gain over prior adaptive agent methods. Our code and model are available at https://github.com/wangruohui/EfficientVideoAgent.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EVA：面向端到端视频智能体的高效强化学习框架
由于视频序列长、时序依赖复杂且存在冗余帧，基于多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的视频理解仍面临挑战。现有方法通常将MLLMs视为被动识别器，直接处理完整视频或均匀采样帧，缺乏自适应推理能力。近期基于智能体的方法虽引入外部工具，但仍依赖人工设计的工作流程和“先感知后决策”策略，导致长视频处理效率低下。本文提出EVA——一种面向端到端视频智能体的高效强化学习框架，通过迭代式的“摘要-规划-行动-反思”推理机制实现“先规划后感知”。EVA能自主决策观看内容、时机与方式，实现查询驱动的高效视频理解。为训练此类智能体，我们设计了一个简洁有效的三阶段学习流程：监督微调（SFT）、卡尼曼-特沃斯基优化（KTO）与广义奖励策略优化（GRPO），衔接监督模仿与强化学习。我们进一步构建了各阶段的高质量数据集，支持稳定可复现的训练。在六个视频理解基准测试中，EVA展现出全面能力：相比通用MLLM基线提升6-12%，较现有自适应智能体方法再提升1-3%。代码与模型已开源：https://github.com/wangruohui/EfficientVideoAgent。

For training, they introduce a three-stage pipeline combining supervised fine-tuning, Kahneman-Tversky Optimization, and Generalized Reward Policy Optimization, supported by high-quality datasets. Experimental results on six benchmarks show that EVA outperforms general MLLM baselines by 6-12% and prior adaptive agent methods by an additional 1-3%, demonstrating comprehensive video understanding capabilities.

Hybrid Stackelberg Game and Diffusion-based Auction for Two-tier Agentic AI Task Offloading in Internet of Agents
Authors: Yue Zhong, Yongju Tong, Jiawen Kang, Minghui Dai, Hong-Ning Dai, Zhou Su, Dusit Niyato
First: 2025-11-27T03:55:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T07:47:51+00:00
Comments: Revisions are needed
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Internet of Agents (IoA) is rapidly gaining prominence as a foundational architecture for interconnected intelligent systems, designed to facilitate seamless discovery, communication, and collaborative reasoning among a vast network of Artificial Intelligence (AI) agents. Powered by Large Language and Vision-Language Models, IoA enables the development of interactive, rational agents capable of complex cooperation, moving far beyond traditional isolated models. IoA involves physical entities, i.e., Wireless Agents (WAs) with limited onboard resources, which need to offload their compute-intensive agentic AI services to nearby servers. Such servers can be Mobile Agents (MAs), e.g., vehicle agents, or Fixed Agents (FAs), e.g., end-side units agents. Given their fixed geographical locations and stable connectivity, FAs can serve as reliable communication gateways and task aggregation points. This stability allows them to effectively coordinate with and offload to an Aerial Agent (AA) tier, which has an advantage not affordable for highly mobile MAs with dynamic connectivity limitations. As such, we propose a two-tier optimization approach. The first tier employs a multi-leader multi-follower Stackelberg game. In the game, MAs and FAs act as the leaders who set resource prices. WAs are the followers to determine task offloading ratios. However, when FAs become overloaded, they can further offload tasks to available aerial resources. Therefore, the second tier introduces a Double Dutch Auction model where overloaded FAs act as the buyers to request resources, and AAs serve as the sellers for resource provision. We then develop a diffusion-based Deep Reinforcement Learning algorithm to solve the model. Numerical results demonstrate the superiority of our proposed scheme in facilitating task offloading.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于混合斯塔克尔伯格博弈与扩散拍卖的智能体互联网双层任务卸载机制
智能体互联网（IoA）作为互联智能系统的基础架构正迅速崛起，其通过大语言与视觉语言模型驱动，使智能体能够实现远超传统孤立模型的复杂协同交互。IoA中的无线智能体（WA）因本地资源有限，需将计算密集型AI服务卸载至邻近服务器——移动智能体（MA，如车载智能体）或固定智能体（FA，如边缘单元智能体）。FA凭借地理位置固定与连接稳定的特性，可作为可靠通信网关与任务聚合节点，并进一步协调卸载至具有动态连接优势的空中智能体（AA）层。为此，本文提出双层优化方案：第一层采用多领导者-多追随者斯塔克尔伯格博弈，MA与FA作为领导者制定资源价格，WA作为追随者确定任务卸载比例；当FA过载时，第二层启动荷兰式双重拍卖模型，过载FA作为买方请求资源，AA作为卖方提供资源。本文进一步设计基于扩散的深度强化学习算法求解模型，数值结果验证了所提方案在促进任务卸载方面的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for efficient task offloading in the Internet of Agents (IoA), where resource-constrained Wireless Agents (WAs) must offload compute-intensive AI services to nearby servers, such as Mobile Agents (MAs) or Fixed Agents (FAs), with FAs further able to offload to Aerial Agents (AAs) due to their stability. The method proposes a two-tier optimization: first, a multi-leader multi-follower Stackelberg game where MAs and FAs set resource prices and WAs determine offloading ratios; second, a Double Dutch Auction model for overloaded FAs to request resources from AAs, solved using a diffusion-based Deep Reinforcement Learning algorithm. Experimental results from numerical simulations demonstrate the scheme's superiority in facilitating effective task offloading within the IoA framework.
本文的动机是在智能体互联网（IoA）中实现高效的任务卸载，其中资源受限的无线智能体（WAs）需要将计算密集的AI服务卸载到附近的服务器，如移动智能体（MAs）或固定智能体（FAs），而FAs由于其稳定性可进一步卸载任务到空中智能体（AAs）。方法上提出了一种双层优化：第一层采用多领导者多跟随者的Stackelberg博弈，其中MAs和FAs设定资源价格，WAs决定卸载比例；第二层引入双荷兰拍卖模型，让过载的FAs作为买家向作为卖家的AAs请求资源，并通过基于扩散的深度强化学习算法求解模型。数值实验结果表明，该方案在促进IoA中的任务卸载方面具有优越性。
VLM-CAD: VLM-Optimized Collaborative Agent Design Workflow for Analog Circuit Sizing
Authors: Guanyuan Pan, Shuai Wang, Yugui Lin, Tiansheng Zhou, Pietro Liò, Zhenxin Zhao, Yaqi Wang
Venue: ACMMM 2026
First: 2026-01-12T08:37:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T07:44:42+00:00
Comments: submitted to the 34th ACM International Conference on Multimedia (ACMMM 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision Language Models (VLMs) have demonstrated remarkable potential in multimodal reasoning, yet they inherently suffer from spatial blindness and logical hallucinations when interpreting densely structured engineering content, such as analog circuit schematics. To address these challenges, we propose a Vision Language Model-Optimized Collaborative Agent Design Workflow for Analog Circuit Sizing (VLM-CAD) designed for robust, step-by-step reasoning over multimodal evidence. VLM-CAD bridges the modality gap by integrating a neuro-symbolic structural parsing module, Image2Net, which transforms raw pixels into explicit topological graphs and structured JSON representations to anchor VLM interpretation in deterministic facts. To ensure the reliability required for engineering decisions, we further propose ExTuRBO, an Explainable Trust Region Bayesian Optimization method. ExTuRBO serves as an explainable grounding engine, employing agent-generated semantic seeds to warm-start local searches and utilizing Automatic Relevance Determination to provide quantified evidence for the VLM's decisions. Experimental results on two complex circuit benchmarks demonstrate that VLM-CAD significantly enhances spatial reasoning accuracy and maintains physics-based explainability. VLM-CAD consistently satisfies complex specification requirements while achieving low power consumption, with a total runtime under 66 minutes, marking a significant step toward robust, explainable multimodal reasoning in specialized technical domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VLM-CAD：面向模拟电路尺寸优化的视觉语言模型协同智能体设计工作流
视觉语言模型在多模态推理中展现出显著潜力，但在解析模拟电路原理图等密集结构化工程内容时，存在固有的空间盲区与逻辑幻觉问题。为应对这些挑战，我们提出一种面向模拟电路尺寸优化的视觉语言模型协同智能体设计工作流，旨在实现基于多模态证据的鲁棒性分步推理。该工作流通过集成神经符号结构解析模块Image2Net来弥合模态鸿沟，该模块将原始像素转换为显式拓扑图与结构化JSON表示，从而将视觉语言模型解释锚定于确定性事实。为确保工程决策所需的可靠性，我们进一步提出可解释信任域贝叶斯优化方法，该方法作为可解释的 grounding 引擎，利用智能体生成的语义种子热启动局部搜索，并采用自动相关性判定为视觉语言模型决策提供量化证据。在两个复杂电路基准测试上的实验结果表明，该工作流显著提升了空间推理精度并保持基于物理解释性，在满足复杂规格要求的同时实现低功耗，总运行时间低于66分钟，标志着专业技术领域向鲁棒可解释多模态推理迈出重要一步。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the spatial blindness and logical hallucinations of Vision Language Models (VLMs) when interpreting complex analog circuit schematics, which hinders reliable engineering design. The proposed method, VLM-CAD, integrates a neuro-symbolic structural parsing module called Image2Net to convert circuit images into explicit topological graphs and structured JSON, anchoring VLM reasoning in factual data, and employs ExTuRBO, an Explainable Trust Region Bayesian Optimization method, to warm-start searches and provide quantified evidence for decisions. Experimental results on two circuit benchmarks show that VLM-CAD significantly improves spatial reasoning accuracy, maintains physics-based explainability, consistently meets complex specifications with low power consumption, and completes sizing within 66 minutes, advancing robust multimodal reasoning in technical domains.
本工作的动机是解决视觉语言模型在解释复杂模拟电路原理图时存在的空间盲区和逻辑幻觉问题，这些问题阻碍了可靠的工程设计。所提出的VLM-CAD方法集成了一个名为Image2Net的神经符号结构解析模块，将电路图像转换为显式的拓扑图和结构化JSON，使VLM推理基于确定性事实，并采用可解释信任域贝叶斯优化方法ExTuRBO来热启动局部搜索并为决策提供量化证据。在两个电路基准上的实验结果表明，VLM-CAD显著提高了空间推理准确性，保持了基于物理解释性，始终满足复杂规格要求且功耗低，总运行时间在66分钟内，推动了专业技术领域中稳健的多模态推理发展。
VLGOR: Visual-Language Knowledge Guided Offline Reinforcement Learning for Generalizable Agents
Authors: Pengsen Liu, Maosen Zeng, Nan Tang, Kaiyuan Li, Jing-Cheng Pang, Yunan Liu, Yang Yu
First: 2026-03-24T07:40:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T07:40:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Combining Large Language Models (LLMs) with Reinforcement Learning (RL) enables agents to interpret language instructions more effectively for task execution. However, LLMs typically lack direct perception of the physical environment, which limits their understanding of environmental dynamics and their ability to generalize to unseen tasks. To address this limitation, we propose Visual-Language Knowledge-Guided Offline Reinforcement Learning (VLGOR), a framework that integrates visual and language knowledge to generate imaginary rollouts, thereby enriching the interaction data. The core premise of VLGOR is to fine-tune a vision-language model to predict future states and actions conditioned on an initial visual observation and high-level instructions, ensuring that the generated rollouts remain temporally coherent and spatially plausible. Furthermore, we employ counterfactual prompts to produce more diverse rollouts for offline RL training, enabling the agent to acquire knowledge that facilitates following language instructions while grounding in environments based on visual cues. Experiments on robotic manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that VLGOR significantly improves performance on unseen tasks requiring novel optimal policies, achieving a success rate over 24% higher than the baseline methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VLGOR：面向可泛化智能体的视觉-语言知识引导离线强化学习
将大语言模型与强化学习结合，可使智能体更有效地解析语言指令以执行任务。然而，大语言模型通常缺乏对物理环境的直接感知，这限制了其对环境动态的理解以及向未见任务泛化的能力。为突破此限制，我们提出视觉-语言知识引导离线强化学习框架，通过融合视觉与语言知识生成模拟交互轨迹，从而丰富交互数据。VLGOR的核心前提是微调视觉-语言模型，使其能基于初始视觉观测与高层级指令预测未来状态与动作，确保生成的轨迹保持时间连贯性与空间合理性。此外，我们采用反事实提示生成更多样化的轨迹用于离线强化学习训练，使智能体能够获取基于视觉线索理解环境、并遵循语言指令的知识。在机器人操作基准测试上的实验表明，VLGOR在需要新最优策略的未见任务上性能显著提升，成功率较基线方法提高超过24%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to enhance the generalization capabilities of agents in unseen tasks by addressing the limitation of Large Language Models (LLMs) in directly perceiving and understanding physical environments. The method introduces VLGOR, a framework that integrates visual and language knowledge to generate temporally coherent and spatially plausible imaginary rollouts, using a fine-tuned vision-language model conditioned on initial observations and instructions, along with counterfactual prompts to increase diversity. Main experimental results on robotic manipulation benchmarks show that VLGOR significantly outperforms baseline methods, achieving over a 24% higher success rate in tasks requiring novel optimal policies.
本研究的动机是通过解决大语言模型在直接感知和理解物理环境方面的局限性，来提升智能体在未见任务中的泛化能力。方法上提出了VLGOR框架，该框架整合视觉与语言知识，通过微调视觉语言模型，基于初始视觉观察和高级指令生成时间连贯且空间合理的想象轨迹，并利用反事实提示增加轨迹多样性以用于离线强化学习训练。主要实验结果在机器人操作基准测试中表明，VLGOR显著优于基线方法，在需要新最优策略的任务上成功率提高了超过24%。
Grounding Sim-to-Real Generalization in Dexterous Manipulation: An Empirical Study with Vision-Language-Action Models
Authors: Ruixing Jin, Zicheng Zhu, Ruixiang Ouyang, Sheng Xu, Bo Yue, Zhizheng Wu, Guiliang Liu
First: 2026-03-24T07:21:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T07:21:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning a generalist control policy for dexterous manipulation typically relies on large-scale datasets. Given the high cost of real-world data collection, a practical alternative is to generate synthetic data through simulation. However, the resulting synthetic data often exhibits a significant gap from real-world distributions. While many prior studies have proposed algorithms to bridge the Sim-to-Real discrepancy, there remains a lack of principled research that grounds these methods in real-world manipulation tasks, particularly their performance on generalist policies such as Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models. In this study, we empirically examine the primary determinants of Sim-to-Real generalization across four dimensions: multi-level domain randomization, photorealistic rendering, physics-realistic modeling, and reinforcement learning updates. To support this study, we design a comprehensive evaluation protocol to quantify the real-world performance of manipulation tasks. The protocol accounts for key variations in background, lighting, distractors, object types, and spatial features. Through experiments involving over 10k real-world trials, we derive critical insights into Sim-to-Real transfer. To inform and advance future studies, we release both the robotic platforms and the evaluation protocol for public access to facilitate independent verification, thereby establishing a realistic and standardized benchmark for dexterous manipulation policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：灵巧操作中仿真到现实泛化的实证研究：基于视觉-语言-动作模型
学习灵巧操作的通用控制策略通常依赖大规模数据集。鉴于真实世界数据采集成本高昂，一种实用替代方案是通过仿真生成合成数据。然而，合成数据常与现实世界分布存在显著差异。尽管已有许多研究提出算法以弥合仿真到现实的差异，但缺乏将这些方法扎根于真实操作任务的原则性研究，尤其是对视觉-语言-动作模型等通用策略的性能评估。本研究通过实证从四个维度检验仿真到现实泛化的关键决定因素：多层级域随机化、逼真渲染、物理真实建模及强化学习更新。为此，我们设计了综合评估协议以量化操作任务在现实世界的性能，涵盖背景、光照、干扰物、物体类型和空间特征等关键变量。通过超过一万次真实世界试验，我们得出仿真到现实迁移的重要结论。为促进未来研究，我们公开机器人平台与评估协议以供独立验证，从而为灵巧操作策略建立现实且标准化的基准。

This paper is motivated by the challenge of bridging the simulation-to-reality gap for training generalist dexterous manipulation policies, specifically Vision-Language-Action models, where real-world data is costly. The method involves an empirical study examining four key determinants of generalization: multi-level domain randomization, photorealistic rendering, physics-realistic modeling, and reinforcement learning updates, supported by a comprehensive evaluation protocol that accounts for variations in background, lighting, and objects. The main experimental results, derived from over 10,000 real-world trials, provide critical insights into Sim-to-Real transfer, and the authors release their robotic platforms and protocol to establish a standardized benchmark for future research.
本文的研究动机在于解决训练通用灵巧操作策略（特别是视觉-语言-动作模型）时面临的仿真到现实差距问题，因为真实世界数据收集成本高昂。研究方法是通过实证分析，从多层次域随机化、逼真渲染、物理真实建模和强化学习更新四个维度考察泛化性能的关键因素，并设计了一个考虑背景、光照和物体变化等的综合评估协议。主要实验结果基于超过一万次真实世界试验，得出了关于仿真到现实迁移的重要见解，作者还公开了机器人平台和评估协议，旨在为未来研究建立一个现实且标准化的基准。
MJ1: Multimodal Judgment via Grounded Verification
Authors: Bhavesh Kumar, Dylan Feng, Leonard Tang
First: 2026-03-09T05:55:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T06:52:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal judges struggle to ground decisions in visual evidence. We present MJ1, a multimodal judge trained with reinforcement learning that enforces visual grounding through a structured grounded verification chain (observations $\rightarrow$ claims $\rightarrow$ verification $\rightarrow$ evaluation $\rightarrow$ scoring) and a counterfactual consistency reward that penalizes position bias. Even without training, our mechanism improves base-model accuracy on MMRB2 by +3.8 points on Image Editing and +1.7 on Multimodal Reasoning. After training, MJ1, with only 3B active parameters, achieves 77.0% accuracy on MMRB2 and surpasses orders-of-magnitude larger models like Gemini-3-Pro. These results show that grounded verification and consistency-based training substantially improve multimodal judgment without increasing model scale.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MJ1：基于视觉验证的多模态判断模型
多模态判断模型常难以将决策基于视觉证据。我们提出MJ1，一种通过强化学习训练的多模态判断模型，采用结构化视觉验证链（观察→主张→验证→评估→评分）确保视觉依据，并通过反事实一致性奖励机制减少立场偏差。未经训练时，该机制在MMRB2基准上使基础模型在图像编辑任务准确率提升3.8点，多模态推理提升1.7点。训练后，仅含30亿激活参数的MJ1在MMRB2准确率达77.0%，超越Gemini-3-Pro等规模大数个量级的模型。结果表明，视觉验证与一致性训练能显著提升多模态判断能力，且无需扩大模型规模。
