TREX: Trajectory Explanations for Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dilina Rajapakse, Juan C. Rosero, Ivana Dusparic
First: 2026-03-23T13:55:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T13:55:14+00:00
Comments: Accepted by 4th World Conference on eXplainable Artificial Intelligence
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has demonstrated its ability to solve complex decision-making problems in a variety of domains, by optimizing reward signals obtained through interaction with an environment. However, many real-world scenarios involve multiple, potentially conflicting objectives that cannot be easily represented by a single scalar reward. Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning (MORL) addresses this limitation by enabling agents to optimize several objectives simultaneously, explicitly reasoning about trade-offs between them. However, the ``black box" nature of the RL models makes the decision process behind chosen objective trade-offs unclear. Current Explainable Reinforcement Learning (XRL) methods are typically designed for single scalar rewards and do not account for explanations with respect to distinct objectives or user preferences. To address this gap, in this paper we propose TREX, a Trajectory based Explainability framework to explain Multi-objective Reinforcement Learning policies, based on trajectory attribution. TREX generates trajectories directly from the learned expert policy, across different user preferences and clusters them into semantically meaningful temporal segments. We quantify the influence of these behavioural segments on the Pareto trade-off by training complementary policies that exclude specific clusters, measuring the resulting relative deviation on the observed rewards and actions compared to the original expert policy. Experiments on multi-objective MuJoCo environments - HalfCheetah, Ant and Swimmer, demonstrate the framework's ability to isolate and quantify the specific behavioural patterns.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TREX：多目标强化学习的轨迹解释框架
强化学习（RL）通过优化与环境交互获得的奖励信号，已证明其解决各领域复杂决策问题的能力。然而，许多现实场景涉及多个可能相互冲突的目标，难以用单一标量奖励表示。多目标强化学习（MORL）通过使智能体同时优化多个目标并显式权衡其关系来应对这一局限。但RL模型的“黑盒”特性使得目标权衡的决策过程不透明。当前可解释强化学习（XRL）方法通常针对单一标量奖励设计，无法提供针对不同目标或用户偏好的解释。为填补这一空白，本文提出基于轨迹归因的TREX框架，用于解释多目标强化学习策略。TREX直接从学习到的专家策略生成轨迹，覆盖不同用户偏好，并将其聚类为具有语义意义的时间片段。通过训练排除特定聚类片段的互补策略，测量其与原始专家策略在观测奖励和行动上的相对偏差，量化这些行为片段对帕累托权衡的影响。在多目标MuJoCo环境（HalfCheetah、Ant和Swimmer）上的实验验证了该框架分离和量化特定行为模式的能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to explain the trade-off decisions made by Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning (MORL) agents, which optimize multiple conflicting objectives, as existing explainable RL methods are designed for single scalar rewards and lack transparency for distinct objectives or user preferences. The proposed method, TREX, is a trajectory-based explainability framework that generates trajectories from a learned expert policy across various user preferences, clusters them into meaningful temporal segments, and quantifies each segment's influence on the Pareto trade-off by training complementary policies that exclude specific clusters to measure deviations in rewards and actions. Experimental results on multi-objective MuJoCo environments (HalfCheetah, Ant, and Swimmer) demonstrate that TREX can effectively isolate and quantify specific behavioral patterns underlying the policy's objective trade-offs.
本文的动机在于需要解释多目标强化学习（MORL）智能体在优化多个冲突目标时所做的权衡决策，因为现有的可解释强化学习方法专为单一标量奖励设计，缺乏针对不同目标或用户偏好的透明度。所提出的方法TREX是一个基于轨迹的可解释性框架，它从学习到的专家策略中生成不同用户偏好下的轨迹，将其聚类为有意义的时序片段，并通过训练排除特定片段的互补策略来测量奖励和行动的相对偏差，从而量化每个片段对帕累托权衡的影响。在多目标MuJoCo环境（HalfCheetah、Ant和Swimmer）上的实验结果表明，TREX能够有效隔离并量化策略目标权衡背后的具体行为模式。
Demystifying Reinforcement Learning for Long-Horizon Tool-Using Agents: A Comprehensive Recipe
Authors: Xixi Wu, Qianguo Sun, Ruiyang Zhang, Chao Song, Junlong Wu, Yiyan Qi, Hong Cheng
First: 2026-03-23T13:40:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T13:40:08+00:00
Comments: Codes are available at https://github.com/WxxShirley/Agent-STAR
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) is essential for evolving Large Language Models (LLMs) into autonomous agents capable of long-horizon planning, yet a practical recipe for scaling RL in complex, multi-turn environments remains elusive. This paper presents a systematic empirical study using TravelPlanner, a challenging testbed requiring tool orchestration to satisfy multifaceted constraints. We decompose the agentic RL design space along 5 axes: reward shaping, model scaling, data composition, algorithm selection, and environmental stability. Our controlled experiments yield 7 key takeaways, e.g., (1) reward and algorithm choices are scale-dependent as smaller models benefit from staged rewards and enhanced exploration, whereas larger models converge efficiently with simpler dense rewards, (2) ~ 1K training samples with a balanced difficulty mixture mark a sweet spot for both in-domain and out-of-domain performance, and (3) environmental stability is critical to prevent policy degradation. Based on our distilled recipe, our RL-trained models achieve state-of-the-art performance on TravelPlanner, significantly outperforming leading LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：揭秘长时程工具使用智能体的强化学习：一套完整方案
强化学习（RL）对于将大语言模型（LLMs）进化为具备长时程规划能力的自主智能体至关重要，然而在复杂多轮环境中扩展RL的实用方案仍不明确。本文通过TravelPlanner（一个需要工具编排以满足多维度约束的挑战性测试平台）开展系统性实证研究。我们将智能体RL设计空间分解为5个维度：奖励塑形、模型缩放、数据构成、算法选择和环境稳定性。控制实验得出7项关键发现，例如：（1）奖励与算法选择具有规模依赖性——较小模型受益于分阶段奖励和增强探索，而较大模型通过简单密集奖励即可高效收敛；（2）约1K个难度均衡的训练样本构成领域内外性能的最佳平衡点；（3）环境稳定性对防止策略退化至关重要。基于提炼的方案，我们经RL训练的模型在TravelPlanner上达到最先进性能，显著超越主流LLMs。

BioBO: Biology-informed Bayesian Optimization for Perturbation Design
Authors: Yanke Li, Tianyu Cui, Tommaso Mansi, Mangal Prakash, Rui Liao
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-24T10:50:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T12:43:41+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Efficient design of genomic perturbation experiments is crucial for accelerating drug discovery and therapeutic target identification, yet exhaustive perturbation of the human genome remains infeasible due to the vast search space of potential genetic interactions and experimental constraints. Bayesian optimization (BO) has emerged as a powerful framework for selecting informative interventions, but existing approaches often fail to exploit domain-specific biological prior knowledge. We propose Biology-Informed Bayesian Optimization (BioBO), a method that integrates Bayesian optimization with multimodal gene embeddings and enrichment analysis, a widely used tool for gene prioritization in biology, to enhance surrogate modeling and acquisition strategies. BioBO combines biologically grounded priors with acquisition functions in a principled framework, which biases the search toward promising genes while maintaining the ability to explore uncertain regions. Through experiments on established public benchmarks and datasets, we demonstrate that BioBO improves labeling efficiency by 25-40%, and consistently outperforms conventional BO by identifying top-performing perturbations more effectively. Moreover, by incorporating enrichment analysis, BioBO yields pathway-level explanations for selected perturbations, offering mechanistic interpretability that links designs to biologically coherent regulatory circuits.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BioBO：面向扰动设计的生物学信息贝叶斯优化方法
基因组扰动实验的高效设计对加速药物发现和治疗靶点识别至关重要，但由于潜在遗传相互作用的巨大搜索空间和实验限制，对人类基因组进行穷举扰动仍不可行。贝叶斯优化已成为选择信息性干预的有力框架，但现有方法往往未能利用特定领域的生物学先验知识。我们提出生物学信息贝叶斯优化方法，该方法将贝叶斯优化与多模态基因嵌入及富集分析相结合——后者是生物学中广泛使用的基因优先级排序工具——以增强代理模型和采集策略。BioBO在原则性框架中将生物学基础先验与采集函数相结合，使搜索偏向有前景的基因，同时保持探索不确定区域的能力。通过在已建立的公共基准和数据集上的实验，我们证明BioBO将标记效率提升25-40%，并通过更有效地识别高性能扰动持续优于传统贝叶斯优化。此外，通过整合富集分析，BioBO能为所选扰动提供通路层面的解释，提供将设计与生物学连贯调控回路相联系的机制可解释性。

Deep Reinforcement Learning and The Tale of Two Temporal Difference Errors
Authors: Juan Sebastian Rojas, Chi-Guhn Lee
First: 2026-03-23T12:43:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T12:43:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The temporal difference (TD) error was first formalized in Sutton (1988), where it was first characterized as the difference between temporally successive predictions, and later, in that same work, formulated as the difference between a bootstrapped target and a prediction. Since then, these two interpretations of the TD error have been used interchangeably in the literature, with the latter eventually being adopted as the standard critic loss in deep reinforcement learning (RL) architectures. In this work, we show that these two interpretations of the TD error are not always equivalent. In particular, we show that increasingly-nonlinear deep RL architectures can cause these interpretations of the TD error to yield increasingly different numerical values. Then, building on this insight, we show how choosing one interpretation of the TD error over the other can affect the performance of deep RL algorithms that utilize the TD error to compute other quantities, such as with deep differential (i.e., average-reward) RL methods. All in all, our results show that the default interpretation of the TD error as the difference between a bootstrapped target and a prediction does not always hold in deep RL settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：深度强化学习与两种时序差分误差的叙事
时序差分（TD）误差最早由Sutton（1988）形式化提出，最初被定义为时序连续预测之间的差异，随后在同一工作中又被表述为自举目标与预测之间的差值。此后，这两种对TD误差的解释在文献中被交替使用，后者最终被采纳为深度强化学习架构中的标准评论家损失。本研究证明，这两种对TD误差的解释并非总是等效的。具体而言，我们揭示了日益非线性的深度强化学习架构会导致这两种解释产生逐渐增大的数值差异。基于此发现，我们进一步论证了在深度强化学习算法中（例如采用深度差分（即平均奖励）强化学习方法时），选择不同的TD误差解释将如何影响依赖TD误差计算其他量的算法性能。总体而言，我们的研究结果表明，将TD误差默认为自举目标与预测之差的做法在深度强化学习场景中并不总是成立。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the two historical interpretations of the temporal difference (TD) error in the context of deep reinforcement learning, motivated by their widespread but potentially interchangeable use in the literature. The method involves analyzing how increasingly nonlinear deep neural network architectures cause these two interpretations—the difference between successive predictions versus the difference between a bootstrapped target and a prediction—to diverge numerically. The main experimental results demonstrate that this divergence significantly impacts algorithm performance, particularly in deep differential reinforcement learning methods, revealing that the standard bootstrapped-target interpretation is not universally reliable in deep RL settings.
本文研究了深度强化学习中时间差分误差的两种历史解释，动机源于文献中广泛但可能互换地使用这两种定义。方法上，论文分析了日益非线性的深度神经网络架构如何导致这两种解释——即连续预测之间的差异与自举目标与预测之间的差异——在数值上产生分歧。主要实验结果表明，这种分歧显著影响了算法性能，特别是在深度差分强化学习方法中，揭示了标准的自举目标解释在深度强化学习环境中并不总是成立。
P^2O: Joint Policy and Prompt Optimization
Authors: Xinyu Lu, Kaiqi Zhang, Jinglin Yang, Boxi Cao, Yaojie Lu, Hongyu Lin, Min He, Xianpei Han, Le Sun
First: 2026-03-23T12:08:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T12:08:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, vanilla RLVR suffers from inefficient exploration, particularly when confronting "hard samples" that yield nearzero success rates. In such scenarios, the reliance on sparse outcome rewards typically results in zero-advantage estimates, effectively starving the model of supervision signals despite the high informational value of these instances. To address this, we propose P^2O, a novel framework that synergizes Prompt Optimization with Policy Optimization. P^2O identifies hard samples during training iterations and leverages the GeneticPareto (GEPA) prompt optimization algorithm to evolve prompt templates that guide the model toward discovering successful trajectories. Crucially, unlike traditional prompt engineering methods that rely on input augmentation, P^2O distills the reasoning gains induced by these optimized prompts directly into the model parameters. This mechanism provides denser positive supervision signals for hard samples and accelerates convergence. Extensive experiments demonstrate that P^2O not only achieves superior performance on in-distribution datasets but also exhibits strong generalization, yielding substantial improvements on out-of-distribution benchmarks (+4.7% avg.).
中文标题/摘要
标题：P^2O：联合策略与提示优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已成为增强大语言模型推理能力的重要范式。然而，传统RLVR存在探索效率低下的问题，尤其在面对成功率趋近于零的“困难样本”时。此类场景下，稀疏结果奖励通常导致优势估计为零，使模型难以从这些高信息价值样本中获得有效监督信号。为此，我们提出P^2O框架，将提示优化与策略优化协同整合。该框架在训练迭代中识别困难样本，并利用遗传帕累托提示优化算法进化提示模板，引导模型发现成功轨迹。与传统依赖输入增强的提示工程方法不同，P^2O将优化提示产生的推理增益直接蒸馏至模型参数中。该机制为困难样本提供更密集的正向监督信号，加速收敛过程。大量实验表明，P^2O不仅在分布内数据集上取得更优性能，还展现出强泛化能力，在分布外基准测试中实现显著提升（平均+4.7%）。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficient exploration problem in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for Large Language Models, particularly when dealing with hard samples that yield near-zero success rates and sparse rewards. To solve this, the authors propose P^2O, a framework that jointly optimizes policy and prompts by identifying hard samples during training and using a GeneticPareto algorithm to evolve prompt templates that guide the model toward successful trajectories, then distilling these reasoning gains into model parameters for denser supervision. Experimental results show that P^2O achieves superior performance on in-distribution datasets and strong generalization, with an average improvement of +4.7% on out-of-distribution benchmarks.
该论文针对大型语言模型的可验证奖励强化学习中探索效率低下的问题，特别是在处理成功率接近零、奖励稀疏的困难样本时。为解决此问题，作者提出了P^2O框架，通过联合优化策略和提示，在训练中识别困难样本，并利用遗传帕累托算法进化提示模板以引导模型找到成功轨迹，然后将这些推理收益蒸馏到模型参数中以提供更密集的监督信号。实验结果表明，P^2O在分布内数据集上取得了优异性能，并展现出强大的泛化能力，在分布外基准测试中平均提升了4.7%。
Manifold-Aware Exploration for Reinforcement Learning in Video Generation
Authors: Mingzhe Zheng, Weijie Kong, Yue Wu, Dengyang Jiang, Yue Ma, Xuanhua He, Bin Lin, Kaixiong Gong, Zhao Zhong, Liefeng Bo, Qifeng Chen, Harry Yang
First: 2026-03-23T12:04:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T12:04:38+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 12 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) methods for video generation like FlowGRPO remain far less reliable than their counterparts for language models and images. This gap arises because video generation has a complex solution space, and the ODE-to-SDE conversion used for exploration can inject excess noise, lowering rollout quality and making reward estimates less reliable, which destabilizes post-training alignment. To address this problem, we view the pre-trained model as defining a valid video data manifold and formulate the core problem as constraining exploration within the vicinity of this manifold, ensuring that rollout quality is preserved and reward estimates remain reliable. We propose SAGE-GRPO (Stable Alignment via Exploration), which applies constraints at both micro and macro levels. At the micro level, we derive a precise manifold-aware SDE with a logarithmic curvature correction and introduce a gradient norm equalizer to stabilize sampling and updates across timesteps. At the macro level, we use a dual trust region with a periodic moving anchor and stepwise constraints so that the trust region tracks checkpoints that are closer to the manifold and limits long-horizon drift. We evaluate SAGE-GRPO on HunyuanVideo1.5 using the original VideoAlign as the reward model and observe consistent gains over previous methods in VQ, MQ, TA, and visual metrics (CLIPScore, PickScore), demonstrating superior performance in both reward maximization and overall video quality. The code and visual gallery are available at https://dungeonmassster.github.io/SAGE-GRPO-Page/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：视频生成强化学习中的流形感知探索方法
针对视频生成的群组相对策略优化（GRPO）方法（如FlowGRPO）的可靠性仍远低于语言模型和图像领域的同类方法。这一差距源于视频生成具有复杂的解空间，且用于探索的ODE至SDE转换可能引入过量噪声，降低生成质量并使奖励估计可靠性下降，进而影响训练后对齐的稳定性。为解决该问题，我们将预训练模型视为定义了一个有效的视频数据流形，并将核心问题转化为约束探索过程使其始终位于该流形邻域内，从而确保生成质量稳定且奖励估计可靠。我们提出SAGE-GRPO（基于稳定探索的对齐方法），在微观与宏观层面同时施加约束：微观层面推导出具有对数曲率修正的精确流形感知SDE，并引入梯度范数均衡器以稳定跨时间步的采样与更新；宏观层面采用双信任区域机制，结合周期性移动锚点与渐进约束，使信任区域追踪更接近流形的检查点并限制长时程漂移。在HunyuanVideo1.5数据集上使用原始VideoAlign作为奖励模型进行评估，SAGE-GRPO在VQ、MQ、TA及视觉指标（CLIPScore、PickScore）上均持续超越现有方法，在奖励最大化与整体视频质量方面均展现优越性能。代码与视觉展示详见https://dungeonmassster.github.io/SAGE-GRPO-Page/。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the instability and poor reliability of existing Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) methods in video generation, which stem from excessive noise injection during exploration that degrades rollout quality and reward estimates. The proposed method, SAGE-GRPO, constrains exploration to stay near the pre-trained model's data manifold through micro-level techniques like a manifold-aware SDE with curvature correction and a gradient norm equalizer, and macro-level dual trust regions with periodic anchors to prevent drift. Experimental results on HunyuanVideo1.5 show consistent improvements over prior methods across video quality (VQ, MQ, TA) and visual metrics (CLIPScore, PickScore), demonstrating enhanced reward maximization and overall video fidelity.
本研究的动机是解决现有群组相对策略优化（GRPO）方法在视频生成中的不稳定性和可靠性差的问题，这些问题源于探索过程中注入的过量噪声会降低生成质量和奖励估计的准确性。所提出的SAGE-GRPO方法通过将探索约束在预训练模型的数据流形附近来解决此问题，具体采用微观层面的技术（如带曲率校正的流形感知随机微分方程和梯度范数均衡器）和宏观层面的双信任区域与周期性锚点来防止漂移。在HunyuanVideo1.5上的实验结果表明，该方法在视频质量指标（VQ、MQ、TA）和视觉指标（CLIPScore、PickScore）上均优于先前方法，实现了更好的奖励最大化和整体视频质量。
Agentic Personas for Adaptive Scientific Explanations with Knowledge Graphs
Authors: Susana Nunes, Tiago Guerreiro, Catia Pesquita
First: 2026-03-23T11:35:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T11:35:40+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
AI explanation methods often assume a static user model, producing non-adaptive explanations regardless of expert goals, reasoning strategies, or decision contexts. Knowledge graph-based explanations, despite their capacity for grounded, path-based reasoning, inherit this limitation. In complex domains such as scientific discovery, this assumption fails to capture the diversity of cognitive strategies and epistemic stances among experts, preventing explanations that foster deeper understanding and informed decision-making. However, the scarcity of human experts limits the use of direct human feedback to produce adaptive explanations. We present a reinforcement learning approach for scientific explanation generation that incorporates agentic personas, structured representations of expert reasoning strategies, that guide the explanation agent towards specific epistemic preferences. In an evaluation of knowledge graph-based explanations for drug discovery, we tested two personas that capture distinct epistemic stances derived from expert feedback. Results show that persona-driven explanations match state-of-the-art predictive performance while persona preferences closely align with those of their corresponding experts. Adaptive explanations were consistently preferred over non-adaptive baselines (n = 22), and persona-based training reduces feedback requirements by two orders of magnitude. These findings demonstrate how agentic personas enable scalable adaptive explainability for AI systems in complex and high-stakes domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于知识图谱的自适应科学解释的代理角色方法
人工智能解释方法通常采用静态用户模型，无论专家目标、推理策略或决策情境如何，均生成非自适应解释。基于知识图谱的解释方法虽具备基于路径的实体推理能力，但仍受此局限。在科学发现等复杂领域中，这种假设无法捕捉专家间认知策略与认知立场的多样性，阻碍了促进深度理解与知情决策的解释生成。然而，人类专家的稀缺性限制了直接利用人工反馈生成自适应解释的可行性。 我们提出一种融合代理角色的强化学习科学解释生成方法，其中代理角色作为专家推理策略的结构化表征，引导解释代理遵循特定认知偏好。在药物发现知识图谱解释的评估中，我们测试了两种从专家反馈中提炼的、代表不同认知立场的代理角色。 结果表明：角色驱动的解释在保持前沿预测性能的同时，其偏好与对应专家高度吻合；自适应解释持续优于非自适应基线（n=22）；基于角色的训练将反馈需求降低两个数量级。这些发现证明代理角色能为复杂高风险领域的人工智能系统提供可扩展的自适应可解释性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitation of static user models in AI explanation methods, which fail to adapt to diverse expert reasoning strategies in complex domains like scientific discovery, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning approach that uses agentic personas—structured representations of expert epistemic preferences—to generate adaptive explanations from knowledge graphs. The method involves training explanation agents guided by specific personas, derived from expert feedback, to produce tailored explanations. In a drug discovery evaluation, results demonstrated that persona-driven explanations achieved state-of-the-art predictive performance, aligned closely with expert preferences, were consistently preferred over non-adaptive baselines by participants, and reduced feedback requirements by two orders of magnitude, showcasing scalable adaptive explainability for high-stakes domains.
针对AI解释方法中静态用户模型无法适应复杂科学发现领域专家多样化推理策略的局限性，本文提出了一种强化学习方法，利用代理角色——即专家认知偏好的结构化表示——来从知识图谱生成自适应解释。该方法通过基于专家反馈衍生的特定角色训练解释代理，以产生定制化解释。在药物发现评估中，结果表明角色驱动的解释达到了最先进的预测性能，与专家偏好紧密对齐，参与者一致倾向于其而非非自适应基线，并将反馈需求降低了两个数量级，展示了在高风险领域可扩展的自适应可解释性。
Towards a Practical Understanding of Lagrangian Methods in Safe Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lindsay Spoor, Álvaro Serra-Gómez, Aske Plaat, Thomas Moerland
First: 2025-10-20T14:13:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T11:11:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Safe reinforcement learning addresses constrained optimization problems where maximizing performance must be balanced against safety constraints, and Lagrangian methods are a widely used approach for this purpose. However, the effectiveness of Lagrangian methods depends crucially on the choice of the Lagrange multiplier $λ$, which governs the multi-objective trade-off between return and cost. A common practice is to update the multiplier automatically during training. Although this approach is standard in practice, there remains limited empirical evidence on the optimally achievable trade-off between return and cost as a function of $λ$, and there is currently no systematic benchmark comparing automated update mechanisms to this empirical optimum. Therefore, we study (i) the constraint geometry for eight widely used safety tasks and (ii) the previously overlooked constraint-regime sensitivity of different Lagrange multiplier update mechanisms in safe reinforcement learning. Through the lens of multi-objective analysis, we present empirical Pareto frontiers that offer a complete visualization of the trade-off between return and cost in the underlying optimization problem. Our results reveal the highly sensitive nature of $λ$ and further show that the restrictiveness of the constraint cost can vary across different cost limits within the same task. This highlights the importance of careful cost limit selection across different regions of cost restrictiveness when evaluating safe reinforcement learning methods. We provide a recommended set of cost limits for each evaluated task and offer an open-source code base: https://github.com/lindsayspoor/Lagrangian_SafeRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向安全强化学习中拉格朗日方法的实践性理解
安全强化学习处理约束优化问题，需在最大化性能与满足安全约束间取得平衡，拉格朗日方法是实现此目标的常用手段。然而，拉格朗日方法的有效性关键取决于拉格朗日乘子$λ$的选择，该乘子主导着回报与成本间的多目标权衡。实践中通常采用训练期间自动更新乘子的方法。尽管这一做法已成标准，但关于$λ$函数所能达到的最优回报-成本权衡仍缺乏充分的实证依据，且目前尚无系统化基准将自动更新机制与此实证最优值进行比较。为此，我们研究：(i) 八种常用安全任务的约束几何特性；(ii) 安全强化学习中不同拉格朗日乘子更新机制先前被忽视的约束机制敏感性。通过多目标分析视角，我们呈现了实证帕累托前沿，完整可视化了底层优化问题中回报与成本的权衡关系。研究结果揭示了$λ$的高度敏感性，并进一步表明同一任务中约束成本的限制性可能随不同成本限值而变化。这凸显了在评估安全强化学习方法时，需针对成本限制性的不同区域谨慎选择成本限值的重要性。我们为每个评估任务提供推荐成本限值集，并开源代码库：https://github.com/lindsayspoor/Lagrangian_SafeRL。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the practical application of Lagrangian methods in safe reinforcement learning, motivated by the need to better understand how the choice of the Lagrange multiplier λ influences the trade-off between maximizing performance and satisfying safety constraints. The method involves a multi-objective analysis, empirically constructing Pareto frontiers to visualize the return-cost trade-off across eight safety tasks, and systematically comparing automated Lagrange multiplier update mechanisms against an empirical optimum. The main experimental results reveal that the effectiveness of λ is highly sensitive, the restrictiveness of constraints can vary significantly with different cost limits within the same task, and the study provides a set of recommended cost limits for benchmarking, underscoring the importance of careful constraint specification in evaluation.
本文研究了拉格朗日方法在安全强化学习中的实际应用，其动机是需要更好地理解拉格朗日乘子λ的选择如何影响最大化性能与满足安全约束之间的权衡。研究方法包括多目标分析，通过经验构建帕累托前沿来可视化八个安全任务中的回报-成本权衡，并系统比较自动拉格朗日乘子更新机制与经验最优解。主要实验结果表明，λ的有效性高度敏感，同一任务中约束的严格性可能随不同成本限制而显著变化，研究为基准测试提供了一套推荐的成本限制，强调了在评估中仔细设定约束条件的重要性。
Native Reasoning Models: Training Language Models to Reason on Unverifiable Data
Authors: Yuanfu Wang, Zhixuan Liu, Xiangtian Li, Chaochao Lu, Chao Yang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-12T04:15:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T10:38:29+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026. Code available at https://github.com/sharkwyf/native-reasoning-models
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The prevailing paradigm for training large reasoning models--combining Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) with Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR)--is fundamentally constrained by its reliance on high-quality, human-annotated reasoning data and external verifiers. This dependency incurs significant data-collection costs, risks embedding human cognitive biases, and confines the reinforcement learning stage to objectively assessable domains like mathematics and coding, leaving a wide range of unverifiable tasks beyond its scope. To overcome these limitations, we introduce NRT (Native Reasoning Training), a novel framework that cultivates complex reasoning by having the model generate its own reasoning traces using only standard question-answer pairs, thereby obviating the need for expert-written demonstrations. NRT reframes the training problem by treating the reasoning process as a latent variable. It employs a unified training objective that models reasoning as an optimization problem, intrinsically rewarding paths that increase the model's likelihood of producing the ground-truth answer. This unified perspective allows us to analyze intrinsic failure modes of prior methods, such as policy collapse, and systematically design more robust reward aggregation functions, creating a self-reinforcing feedback loop where the model learns to think in ways that resolve its own uncertainty. Empirical evaluation on Llama and Mistral model families demonstrates that NRT achieves state-of-the-art performance among verifier-free methods, significantly outperforming standard SFT baselines and prior verifier-free RL methods. Our approach yields particularly strong performance gains in complex reasoning domains and exhibits high robustness to policy collapse, offering a general, scalable path toward building more powerful and broadly applicable reasoning systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：原生推理模型：在不可验证数据上训练语言模型进行推理
当前训练大型推理模型的主流范式——将监督微调（SFT）与可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）相结合——从根本上受限于其对高质量人工标注推理数据和外部验证器的依赖。这种依赖性导致高昂的数据收集成本、可能嵌入人类认知偏见，并将强化学习阶段局限于数学和编程等可客观评估的领域，使大量不可验证任务无法覆盖。为突破这些限制，我们提出NRT（原生推理训练）框架，该框架仅使用标准问答对让模型生成自身推理轨迹，从而无需专家撰写的演示样例，以此培养复杂推理能力。NRT将推理过程视为隐变量重构训练问题，采用统一训练目标将推理建模为优化问题，对提升模型生成正确答案可能性的路径进行内在奖励。这种统一视角使我们能分析先前方法的内在失效模式（如策略崩溃），并系统设计更稳健的奖励聚合函数，形成自我强化的反馈循环，使模型学会通过思考化解自身不确定性。基于Llama和Mistral模型系列的实证评估表明，NRT在无验证器方法中达到最先进性能，显著优于标准SFT基线和先前的无验证器RL方法。该方法在复杂推理领域表现尤为突出，对策略崩溃具有高鲁棒性，为构建更强大、广泛适用的推理系统提供了通用可扩展路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high cost and cognitive bias risks of human-annotated reasoning data and the domain limitation of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, this paper introduces Native Reasoning Training (NRT), a framework that trains language models to reason using only question-answer pairs by treating reasoning as a latent variable and optimizing a unified objective that intrinsically rewards reasoning paths leading to correct answers. The method analyzes and mitigates failure modes like policy collapse through robust reward aggregation, creating a self-reinforcing learning loop. Experimental results on Llama and Mistral models show that NRT achieves state-of-the-art performance among verifier-free methods, outperforming standard supervised fine-tuning and prior verifier-free reinforcement learning approaches, with strong gains in complex reasoning domains and high robustness to collapse.
针对依赖人工标注推理数据的高成本、认知偏见风险以及基于可验证奖励的强化学习领域受限问题，本文提出了原生推理训练（NRT）框架，该方法仅使用问答对训练语言模型进行推理，将推理过程视为隐变量，并通过优化统一目标函数来内在奖励导向正确答案的推理路径。该方法通过设计稳健的奖励聚合函数来分析和缓解策略崩溃等失效模式，形成自我强化的学习循环。在Llama和Mistral模型上的实验结果表明，NRT在无需验证器的方法中达到了最先进的性能，显著优于标准的监督微调基线和先前的无验证器强化学习方法，在复杂推理领域表现突出，且对策略崩溃具有高鲁棒性。
TIC-GRPO: Provable and Efficient Optimization for Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback
Authors: Lei Pang, Jun Luo, Ruinan Jin
First: 2025-08-04T19:01:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T09:37:59+00:00
Comments: 44 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), recently introduced by DeepSeek, is a critic-free reinforcement learning algorithm for fine-tuning large language models. GRPO replaces the value function in Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) with group-normalized rewards while retaining PPO-style token-level importance sampling based on an old policy. Our theoretical analysis reveals that the GRPO update rule estimates the policy gradient at the old policy rather than the current one; however, since the old policy is refreshed every few steps, the resulting discrepancy remains small and the induced bias is negligible in practice. To empirically validate this insight, we conduct an ablation study that entirely removes importance sampling and performs multiple optimization steps using gradients estimated at a fixed old policy. Remarkably, this simplified variant attains performance comparable to standard GRPO. Motivated by this finding, we propose Trajectory-level Importance-Corrected GRPO (TIC-GRPO), a new algorithm that replaces token-level importance ratios with a single trajectory-level probability ratio, thereby yielding an estimate of the current policy gradient while preserving the critic-free structure. Furthermore, we present the first convergence analysis for GRPO-style methods and show that TIC-GRPO converges faster than GRPO. Finally, empirical results across math reasoning and coding tasks demonstrate the superiority of TIC-GRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TIC-GRPO：强化学习人类反馈优化的可证明高效方法
深度求索公司近期提出的组相对策略优化（GRPO）是一种无需价值函数评论家的强化学习算法，用于微调大语言模型。GRPO在保留基于旧策略的PPO风格令牌级重要性采样的同时，用组归一化奖励替代了近端策略优化（PPO）中的价值函数。理论分析表明，GRPO更新规则实际上是在旧策略而非当前策略处估计策略梯度；但由于旧策略每隔数步即更新，实际产生的偏差可忽略不计。为验证该发现，我们进行了消融实验：完全移除重要性采样，仅基于固定旧策略的梯度进行多步优化。值得注意的是，此简化变体取得了与标准GRPO相当的性能。基于此，我们提出轨迹级重要性校正GRPO（TIC-GRPO）新算法，用单一轨迹级概率比替代令牌级重要性比率，从而在保持无评论家结构的同时获得当前策略梯度的估计。此外，我们首次给出GRPO类方法的收敛性分析，证明TIC-GRPO具有更快收敛速度。最终在数学推理与代码生成任务上的实证结果验证了TIC-GRPO的优越性。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to improve the efficiency and theoretical grounding of Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), a critic-free reinforcement learning method for fine-tuning large language models. The authors first analyze GRPO and find its update rule estimates gradients at an old policy, introducing bias, but show through ablation that removing token-level importance sampling yields comparable performance. They then propose TIC-GRPO, which replaces token-level importance ratios with a single trajectory-level probability ratio to estimate the current policy gradient more accurately while remaining critic-free. Experimental results on math reasoning and coding tasks demonstrate TIC-GRPO's superiority, and theoretical analysis confirms it converges faster than GRPO.

DeepCompress: A Dual Reward Strategy for Dynamically Exploring and Compressing Reasoning Chains
Authors: Tian Liang, Wenxiang Jiao, Zhiwei He, Jiahao Xu, Haitao Mi, Dong Yu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-31T12:13:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T09:36:31+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) have demonstrated impressive capabilities but suffer from cognitive inefficiencies like "overthinking" simple problems and "underthinking" complex ones. While existing methods that use supervised fine-tuning (SFT) or reinforcement learning (RL) with token-length rewards can improve efficiency, they often do so at the cost of accuracy. This paper introduces DeepCompress, a novel framework that simultaneously enhances both the accuracy and efficiency of LRMs. We challenge the prevailing approach of consistently favoring shorter reasoning paths, showing that longer responses can contain a broader range of correct solutions for difficult problems. DeepCompress employs an adaptive length reward mechanism that dynamically classifies problems as "Simple" or "Hard" in real-time based on the model's evolving capability. It encourages shorter, more efficient reasoning for "Simple" problems while promoting longer, more exploratory thought chains for "Hard" problems. This dual-reward strategy enables the model to autonomously adjust its Chain-of-Thought (CoT) length, compressing reasoning for well-mastered problems and extending it for those it finds challenging. Experimental results on challenging mathematical benchmarks show that DeepCompress consistently outperforms baseline methods, achieving superior accuracy while significantly improving token efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeepCompress：一种动态探索与压缩推理链的双重奖励策略
大型推理模型（LRMs）虽展现出强大能力，却存在认知效率问题，如对简单问题'过度思考'、对复杂问题'思考不足'。现有方法通过监督微调（SFT）或基于词元长度的强化学习（RL）奖励可提升效率，但常以牺牲准确性为代价。本文提出DeepCompress框架，能同时提升LRMs的准确性与效率。我们挑战了当前普遍推崇短推理路径的做法，证明长响应可能包含更广泛的难题正确解法。DeepCompress采用自适应长度奖励机制，根据模型实时演化的能力动态将问题分类为'简单'或'困难'：对'简单'问题鼓励更短、更高效的推理，对'困难'问题则促进更长、更具探索性的思维链。这种双重奖励策略使模型能自主调整思维链（CoT）长度，压缩已掌握问题的推理过程，并延伸对挑战性问题的思考。在复杂数学基准测试中，DeepCompress持续超越基线方法，在显著提升词元效率的同时获得更优的准确性。

The method employs a dual-reward reinforcement learning strategy with an adaptive length reward mechanism, which dynamically classifies problems as 'Simple' or 'Hard' during training to encourage shorter reasoning paths for simple problems and longer, exploratory chains for hard ones. Experimental results on challenging mathematical benchmarks demonstrate that DeepCompress consistently outperforms baseline methods, achieving superior accuracy while significantly improving token efficiency.

EvoIdeator: Evolving Scientific Ideas through Checklist-Grounded Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Andreas Sauter, Yuyue Zhao, Jacopo Urbani, Wenxiang Hu, Zaiqiao Meng, Lun Zhou, Xiaohui Yan, Yougang Lyu
First: 2026-03-23T09:15:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T09:15:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scientific idea generation is a cornerstone of autonomous knowledge discovery, yet the iterative evolution required to transform initial concepts into high-quality research proposals remains a formidable challenge for Large Language Models (LLMs). Existing Reinforcement Learning (RL) paradigms often rely on rubric-based scalar rewards that provide global quality scores but lack actionable granularity. Conversely, language-based refinement methods are typically confined to inference-time prompting, targeting models that are not explicitly optimized to internalize such critiques. To bridge this gap, we propose \textbf{EvoIdeator}, a framework that facilitates the evolution of scientific ideas by aligning the RL training objective with \textbf{checklist-grounded feedback}. EvoIdeator leverages a structured judge model to generate two synergistic signals: (1) \emph{lexicographic rewards} for multi-dimensional optimization, and (2) \emph{fine-grained language feedback} that offers span-level critiques regarding grounding, feasibility, and methodological rigor. By integrating these signals into the RL loop, we condition the policy to systematically utilize precise feedback during both optimization and inference. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoIdeator, built on Qwen3-4B, significantly outperforms much larger frontier models across key scientific metrics. Crucially, the learned policy exhibits strong generalization to diverse external feedback sources without further fine-tuning, offering a scalable and rigorous path toward self-refining autonomous ideation.

科学思想生成是自主知识发现的基石，但将初始概念迭代演化为高质量研究提案的过程对大语言模型仍具挑战。现有强化学习范式多依赖基于量规的标量奖励，虽提供整体质量评分却缺乏可操作的细粒度指导；而基于语言的改进方法通常局限于推理时提示，未显式优化模型内化此类反馈。为弥合此差距，我们提出EvoIdeator框架，通过将强化学习训练目标与清单式反馈对齐来促进科学思想演化。该框架利用结构化评判模型生成两种协同信号：(1) 用于多维优化的词典序奖励；(2) 提供基础性、可行性及方法论严谨性跨层级批判的细粒度语言反馈。通过将这些信号整合至强化学习循环，我们使策略能在优化和推理阶段系统化利用精准反馈。基于Qwen3-4B的广泛实验表明，EvoIdeator在关键科学指标上显著优于规模更大的前沿模型。尤为重要的是，习得策略无需微调即可泛化至多样化外部反馈源，为自优化自主构思提供了可扩展的严谨路径。

Proximal Policy Optimization in Path Space: A Schrödinger Bridge Perspective
Authors: Yuehu Gong, Zeyuan Wang, Yulin Chen, Yanwei Fu
First: 2026-03-23T06:37:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T06:37:42+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 3figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
On-policy reinforcement learning with generative policies is promising but remains underexplored. A central challenge is that proximal policy optimization (PPO) is traditionally formulated in terms of action-space probability ratios, whereas diffusion- and flow-based policies are more naturally represented as trajectory-level generative processes. In this work, we propose GSB-PPO, a path-space formulation of generative PPO inspired by the Generalized Schrödinger Bridge (GSB). Our framework lifts PPO-style proximal updates from terminal actions to full generation trajectories, yielding a unified view of on-policy optimization for generative policies. Within this framework, we develop two concrete objectives: a clipping-based objective, GSB-PPO-Clip, and a penalty-based objective, GSB-PPO-Penalty. Experimental results show that while both objectives are compatible with on-policy training, the penalty formulation consistently delivers better stability and performance than the clipping counterpart. Overall, our results highlight path-space proximal regularization as an effective principle for training generative policies with PPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：路径空间中的近端策略优化：薛定谔桥视角
基于生成策略的同策略强化学习前景广阔但尚未充分探索。核心挑战在于，传统近端策略优化（PPO）基于动作空间概率比构建，而扩散与流式生成策略更自然地表现为轨迹级生成过程。本研究提出GSB-PPO——一种受广义薛定谔桥（GSB）启发的生成式PPO路径空间框架。该框架将PPO式近端更新从终端动作提升至完整生成轨迹，为生成策略的同策略优化提供了统一视角。在此框架下，我们开发了两个具体目标：基于截断的目标GSB-PPO-Clip与基于惩罚的目标GSB-PPO-Penalty。实验表明，虽然两种目标均适用于同策略训练，但惩罚式目标始终比截断式具有更好的稳定性和性能。总体而言，我们的研究证明了路径空间近端正则化是使用PPO训练生成策略的有效原则。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of applying proximal policy optimization (PPO) to diffusion- and flow-based generative policies, which are naturally defined over trajectories rather than single actions, this paper introduces GSB-PPO, a path-space formulation inspired by the Generalized Schrödinger Bridge. The method lifts PPO's proximal updates from actions to entire generation trajectories, proposing two concrete objectives: a clipping-based version (GSB-PPO-Clip) and a penalty-based version (GSB-PPO-Penalty). Experimental results demonstrate that both objectives enable on-policy training, but the penalty formulation consistently provides superior stability and performance compared to the clipping approach, establishing path-space proximal regularization as an effective principle for training generative policies.
针对近端策略优化（PPO）难以直接应用于基于扩散或流的生成策略（这类策略天然在轨迹层面定义）的挑战，本文受广义薛定谔桥启发，提出了路径空间下的GSB-PPO框架。该方法将PPO的近端更新从单步动作提升至完整生成轨迹，并提出了两种具体目标：基于裁剪的GSB-PPO-Clip和基于惩罚的GSB-PPO-Penalty。实验结果表明，两种目标均支持在线策略训练，但惩罚版本在稳定性和性能上持续优于裁剪版本，从而验证了路径空间近端正则化是训练生成策略的有效原则。
CoVerRL: Breaking the Consensus Trap in Label-Free Reasoning via Generator-Verifier Co-Evolution
Authors: Teng Pan, Yuchen Yan, Zixuan Wang, Ruiqing Zhang, Guiyang Hou, Wenqi Zhang, Weiming Lu, Jun Xiao, Yongliang Shen
First: 2026-03-18T14:38:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T06:36:19+00:00
Comments: Project Page: https://zju-real.github.io/CoVerRL Code: https://github.com/ZJU-REAL/CoVerRL
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
Label-free reinforcement learning enables large language models to improve reasoning capabilities without ground-truth supervision, typically by treating majority-voted answers as pseudo-labels. However, we identify a critical failure mode: as training maximizes self-consistency, output diversity collapses, causing the model to confidently reinforce systematic errors that evade detection. We term this the consensus trap. To escape it, we propose CoVerRL, a framework where a single model alternates between generator and verifier roles, with each capability bootstrapping the other. Majority voting provides noisy but informative supervision for training the verifier, while the improving verifier progressively filters self-consistent errors from pseudo-labels. This co-evolution creates a virtuous cycle that maintains high reward accuracy throughout training. Experiments across Qwen and Llama model families demonstrate that CoVerRL outperforms label-free baselines by 4.7-5.9% on mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Moreover, self-verification accuracy improves from around 55% to over 85%, confirming that both capabilities genuinely co-evolve.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoVerRL：通过生成器-验证器协同进化突破无标签推理中的共识陷阱
无标签强化学习使大语言模型无需真实标注即可提升推理能力，通常将多数投票答案作为伪标签。然而我们发现一个关键失效模式：当训练过度追求自洽性时，输出多样性会崩溃，导致模型自信地强化难以察觉的系统性错误——我们称之为共识陷阱。为突破此陷阱，我们提出CoVerRL框架：单一模型在生成器与验证器角色间动态切换，二者能力相互引导提升。多数投票为验证器训练提供带噪声但有信息的监督，而持续优化的验证器逐步从伪标签中过滤自洽性错误。这种协同进化形成良性循环，在训练全程保持高奖励准确率。在Qwen和Llama系列模型上的实验表明，CoVerRL在数学推理基准上比无标签基线提升4.7-5.9%。此外，自我验证准确率从约55%提升至85%以上，证实两种能力真正实现了协同进化。

The paper addresses a critical failure mode in label-free reinforcement learning for large language models, where reliance on majority-voted pseudo-labels leads to a collapse in output diversity and the reinforcement of systematic errors, termed the consensus trap. To overcome this, the authors propose CoVerRL, a framework where a single model alternates between generator and verifier roles, enabling co-evolution: the generator provides majority-voted supervision to train the verifier, while the verifier filters errors from pseudo-labels, creating a virtuous cycle that maintains high reward accuracy. Experimental results on Qwen and Llama model families show CoVerRL outperforms label-free baselines by 4.7-5.9% on mathematical reasoning benchmarks, with self-verification accuracy improving from around 55% to over 85%, confirming effective co-evolution.
本文针对大语言模型在无标签强化学习中的一个关键失败模式，即依赖多数投票伪标签会导致输出多样性崩溃并强化系统性错误，这被称为共识陷阱。为解决此问题，作者提出了CoVerRL框架，其中单个模型在生成器和验证器角色间交替，实现协同进化：生成器通过多数投票提供监督训练验证器，而验证器则过滤伪标签中的错误，形成良性循环以保持高奖励准确性。在Qwen和Llama模型系列上的实验结果表明，CoVerRL在数学推理基准上比无标签基线方法提升了4.7-5.9%，且自验证准确率从约55%提高到超过85%，证实了能力的有效协同进化。
Adaptive Insurance Reserving with CVaR-Constrained Reinforcement Learning under Macroeconomic Regimes
Authors: Stella C. Dong
First: 2025-04-13T01:43:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T06:11:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We develop a reinforcement learning (RL) framework for insurance loss reserving that formulates reserve setting as a finite-horizon sequential decision problem under claim development uncertainty, macroeconomic stress, and solvency governance. The reserving process is modeled as a Markov Decision Process (MDP) in which reserve adjustments influence future reserve adequacy, capital efficiency, and solvency outcomes. A Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) agent is trained using a risk-sensitive reward that penalizes reserve shortfall, capital inefficiency, and breaches of a volatility-adjusted solvency floor, with tail risk explicitly controlled through Conditional Value-at-Risk (CVaR). To reflect regulatory stress-testing practice, the agent is trained under a regime-aware curriculum and evaluated using both regime-stratified simulations and fixed-shock stress scenarios. Empirical results for Workers Compensation and Other Liability illustrate how the proposed RL-CVaR policy improves tail-risk control and reduces solvency violations relative to classical actuarial reserving methods, while maintaining comparable capital efficiency. We further discuss calibration and governance considerations required to align model parameters with firm-specific risk appetite and supervisory expectations under Solvency II and Own Risk and Solvency Assessment (ORSA) frameworks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：宏观经济体制下基于CVaR约束强化学习的自适应保险准备金计提
本文提出了一种用于保险损失准备金计提的强化学习框架，将准备金设定建模为索赔进展不确定性、宏观经济压力与偿付能力监管下的有限时域序贯决策问题。准备金调整过程被构建为马尔可夫决策过程，其中准备金调整会影响未来准备金充足性、资本效率与偿付结果。采用近端策略优化智能体进行训练，其风险敏感型奖励函数对准备金缺口、资本效率低下及波动调整后偿付能力底线的突破进行惩罚，并通过条件风险价值对尾部风险进行显式控制。为反映监管压力测试实践，智能体在体制感知课程下训练，并采用体制分层模拟与固定冲击压力场景进行评估。针对工伤保险与其他责任险的实证结果表明，相较于传统精算准备金方法，所提出的RL-CVaR策略在保持相当资本效率的同时，能提升尾部风险控制并减少偿付能力违规。本文进一步探讨了在偿付能力II与自身风险与偿付能力评估框架下，使模型参数与公司特定风险偏好及监管预期相协调所需的校准与治理考量。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for insurance loss reserving methods that account for claim development uncertainty, macroeconomic stress, and solvency governance, this paper develops a reinforcement learning framework. The method formulates reserving as a Markov Decision Process and trains a Proximal Policy Optimization agent with a risk-sensitive reward that penalizes reserve shortfalls and breaches of a solvency floor, explicitly controlling tail risk using Conditional Value-at-Risk under a regime-aware curriculum. Experimental results on Workers Compensation and Other Liability data show the RL-CVaR policy improves tail-risk control and reduces solvency violations compared to classical actuarial methods while maintaining similar capital efficiency.
本文的动机是开发一种能够考虑索赔发展不确定性、宏观经济压力和偿付能力监管的保险损失准备金计提方法。该方法将准备金计提构建为一个马尔可夫决策过程，并训练一个近端策略优化智能体，其风险敏感奖励函数惩罚准备金短缺和违反偿付能力底线的行为，在考虑宏观经济状态的课程训练下，使用条件风险价值明确控制尾部风险。在 Workers Compensation 和 Other Liability 数据上的实验结果表明，相较于经典的精算方法，所提出的 RL-CVaR 策略改善了尾部风险控制，减少了偿付能力违规，同时保持了可比的资本效率。
CurES: From Gradient Analysis to Efficient Curriculum Learning for Reasoning LLMs
Authors: Yongcheng Zeng, Zexu Sun, Bokai Ji, Erxue Min, Hengyi Cai, Shuaiqiang Wang, Dawei Yin, Haifeng Zhang, Xu Chen, Jun Wang
First: 2025-10-01T15:41:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T06:08:50+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 10 Figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Curriculum learning plays a crucial role in enhancing the training efficiency of large language models (LLMs) on reasoning tasks. However, existing methods often fail to adequately account for variations in prompt difficulty or rely on simplistic filtering mechanisms to select prompt datasets within a narrow criterion range, resulting in significant computational waste. In this work, we approach the problem from the perspective of reinforcement learning gradient optimization, offering a systematic and theoretical investigation into how to improve the training efficiency of LLMs. We identify two key factors influencing training efficiency: the selection of training prompts and the allocation of rollout quantities across different prompts. Our theoretical analysis reveals that the sampling distribution of prompts dictates the convergence rate of gradient descent, while the allocation of the rollout quantity influences the consistency and stability of overall gradient updates. Based on these insights, we propose CurES, an efficient training method that accelerates convergence and employs Bayesian posterior estimation to minimize computational overhead. Experiments demonstrate that our CurES outperforms Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) by +3.30 points and +4.82 points with 1.5B and 7B models, respectively, and exceeds the best prior sample efficient methods by +2.12 points on average across eight math reasoning benchmarks. Additionally, CurES exhibits faster convergence compared to baselines, including GRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CurES：从梯度分析到推理大语言模型的高效课程学习
课程学习在提升大语言模型（LLMs）于推理任务上的训练效率方面起着关键作用。然而，现有方法往往未能充分考虑提示难度的变化，或依赖简单的过滤机制在狭窄的标准范围内选择提示数据集，导致显著的计算资源浪费。本研究从强化学习梯度优化的视角切入，系统性地探讨了如何提升LLMs的训练效率。我们识别出影响训练效率的两个关键因素：训练提示的选择以及不同提示间展开数量的分配。理论分析表明，提示的采样分布决定了梯度下降的收敛速度，而展开数量的分配则影响整体梯度更新的一致性与稳定性。基于这些发现，我们提出了CurES，一种高效训练方法，通过加速收敛并采用贝叶斯后验估计来最小化计算开销。实验证明，CurES在1.5B和7B模型上分别比组相对策略优化（GRPO）高出+3.30分和+4.82分，并在八个数学推理基准测试中平均超越先前最佳样本高效方法+2.12分。此外，与包括GRPO在内的基线方法相比，CurES展现出更快的收敛速度。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational inefficiency of existing curriculum learning methods for reasoning LLMs, which often inadequately address prompt difficulty variations or use simplistic filtering, this paper proposes CurES, a method grounded in reinforcement learning gradient optimization. The approach systematically analyzes how training prompt selection and rollout quantity allocation affect efficiency, finding that prompt sampling distribution influences gradient descent convergence rate while rollout allocation impacts update stability. The proposed CurES method accelerates convergence and uses Bayesian posterior estimation to reduce computational overhead. Experimental results show that CurES outperforms GRPO by up to +4.82 points with 7B models and exceeds prior sample-efficient methods by an average of +2.12 points across eight math reasoning benchmarks, while also demonstrating faster convergence.

A Hybrid Framework for Reinsurance Optimization: Integrating Generative Models and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Stella C. Dong
First: 2025-01-11T02:02:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T06:03:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinsurance optimization is a cornerstone of solvency and capital management, yet traditional approaches often rely on restrictive distributional assumptions and static program designs. We propose a hybrid framework that combines Variational Autoencoders (VAEs) to learn joint distributions of multi-line and multi-year claims data with Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) reinforcement learning to adapt treaty parameters dynamically. The framework explicitly targets expected surplus under capital and ruin-probability constraints, bridging statistical modeling with sequential decision-making. Using simulated and stress-test scenarios, including pandemic-type and catastrophe-type shocks, we show that the hybrid method produces more resilient outcomes than classical proportional and stop-loss benchmarks, delivering higher surpluses and lower tail risk. Our findings highlight the usefulness of generative models for capturing cross-line dependencies and demonstrate the feasibility of RL-based dynamic structuring in practical reinsurance settings. Contributions include (i) clarifying optimization goals in reinsurance RL, (ii) defending generative modeling relative to parametric fits, and (iii) benchmarking against established methods. This work illustrates how hybrid AI techniques can address modern challenges of portfolio diversification, catastrophe risk, and adaptive capital allocation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：再保险优化的混合框架：融合生成模型与强化学习
再保险优化是偿付能力与资本管理的基石，但传统方法常依赖受限的分布假设与静态方案设计。本文提出一种混合框架：通过变分自编码器学习多业务线、多年份理赔数据的联合分布，并采用近端策略优化强化学习动态调整分保合约参数。该框架在资本与破产概率约束下明确优化预期盈余，实现了统计建模与序列决策的衔接。 基于包含疫情型与巨灾型冲击的模拟与压力测试场景，研究表明该混合方法相比传统比例分保与止损分保基准能产生更具韧性的结果，实现更高盈余与更低尾部风险。研究结果凸显了生成模型捕捉跨业务线依赖关系的实用性，并验证了基于强化学习的动态结构设计在实际再保险场景中的可行性。 主要贡献包括：（1）明确再保险强化学习的优化目标；（2）论证生成模型相对于参数拟合的优势；（3）建立与传统方法的对比基准。本工作展示了混合人工智能技术如何应对投资组合分散化、巨灾风险与自适应资本配置等现代挑战。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of traditional reinsurance optimization methods that rely on restrictive assumptions and static designs, this paper proposes a hybrid framework integrating Variational Autoencoders (VAEs) to model joint distributions of claims data and Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) reinforcement learning to dynamically adjust treaty parameters, aiming to maximize expected surplus under capital and ruin-probability constraints. Experimental results on simulated scenarios, including pandemic and catastrophe shocks, demonstrate that this approach outperforms classical proportional and stop-loss benchmarks by achieving higher surpluses and lower tail risk, highlighting the value of generative models for capturing dependencies and the feasibility of RL in practical reinsurance settings.
针对传统再保险优化方法依赖限制性假设和静态设计的不足，本文提出了一种混合框架，结合变分自编码器（VAE）学习多业务线多年份索赔数据的联合分布，并利用近端策略优化（PPO）强化学习动态调整再保险合同参数，以在资本和破产概率约束下最大化期望盈余。在包括疫情型和巨灾型冲击的模拟与压力测试场景中，实验结果表明该方法优于传统的比例再保险和止损再保险基准，实现了更高的盈余和更低的尾部风险，凸显了生成模型捕捉依赖关系的价值以及强化学习在实际再保险环境中的可行性。
Spatio-Temporal Attention Enhanced Multi-Agent DRL for UAV-Assisted Wireless Networks with Limited Communications
Authors: Che Chen, Lanhua Li, Shimin Gong, Yu Zhao, Yuming Fang, Dusit Niyato
First: 2026-03-23T05:42:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T05:42:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we employ multiple UAVs to accelerate data transmissions from ground users (GUs) to a remote base station (BS) via the UAVs' relay communications. The UAVs' intermittent information exchanges typically result in delays in acquiring the complete system state and hinder their effective collaboration. To maximize the overall throughput, we first propose a delay-tolerant multi-agent deep reinforcement learning (MADRL) algorithm that integrates a delay-penalized reward to encourage information sharing among UAVs, while jointly optimizing the UAVs' trajectory planning, network formation, and transmission control strategies. Additionally, considering information loss due to unreliable channel conditions, we further propose a spatio-temporal attention based prediction approach to recover the lost information and enhance each UAV's awareness of the network state. These two designs are envisioned to enhance the network capacity in UAV-assisted wireless networks with limited communications. The simulation results reveal that our new approach achieves over 50\% reduction in information delay and 75% throughput gain compared to the conventional MADRL. Interestingly, it is shown that improving the UAVs' information sharing will not sacrifice the network capacity. Instead, it significantly improves the learning performance and throughput simultaneously. It is also effective in reducing the need for UAVs' information exchange and thus fostering practical deployment of MADRL in UAV-assisted wireless networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向通信受限无人机辅助无线网络的时空注意力增强多智能体深度强化学习
本文利用多架无人机通过中继通信加速地面用户至远程基站的数据传输。无人机间的间歇性信息交换常导致系统状态获取延迟，阻碍其有效协作。为最大化总吞吐量，我们首先提出一种延迟容忍的多智能体深度强化学习算法，通过引入延迟惩罚奖励激励无人机间信息共享，并联合优化无人机轨迹规划、网络组建与传输控制策略。此外，针对信道不可靠导致的信息丢失问题，进一步提出基于时空注意力的预测方法以恢复丢失信息，增强各无人机对网络状态的感知能力。这两项设计旨在提升通信受限的无人机辅助无线网络的容量。仿真结果表明，新方法相比传统多智能体深度强化学习可降低超过50%的信息延迟，并实现75%的吞吐量提升。值得注意的是，增强无人机信息共享不会牺牲网络容量，反而能同步显著提升学习性能与吞吐量。该方法还能有效减少无人机信息交换需求，从而推动多智能体深度强化学习在无人机辅助无线网络中的实际部署。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of maximizing throughput in UAV-assisted wireless networks where limited and delayed communications between UAVs hinder effective collaboration. The authors propose a multi-agent deep reinforcement learning (MADRL) algorithm enhanced with a delay-penalized reward to incentivize timely information sharing among UAVs, jointly optimizing trajectory, network formation, and transmission control. To further counter information loss from unreliable channels, they introduce a spatio-temporal attention mechanism to predict and recover missing state data. Experimental simulations demonstrate that this integrated approach reduces information delay by over 50% and increases throughput by 75% compared to conventional MADRL, showing that improved information sharing enhances both learning performance and network capacity without requiring excessive communication exchanges.
本文针对无人机辅助无线网络中通信受限导致无人机间协作效率低的问题，旨在最大化网络吞吐量。作者提出了一种结合延迟惩罚奖励的多智能体深度强化学习算法，以激励无人机及时共享信息，并联合优化其轨迹规划、网络形成和传输控制策略。此外，为应对不可靠信道造成的信息丢失，还引入了基于时空注意力的预测方法来恢复丢失信息，增强各无人机对网络状态的感知。仿真结果表明，与传统多智能体深度强化学习方法相比，该新方法将信息延迟降低了50%以上，吞吐量提升了75%，证明改进信息共享不仅能同时提升学习性能和网络容量，还能减少对频繁通信的依赖，有利于实际部署。
Dynamic Reinsurance Treaty Bidding via Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Stella C. Dong, James R. Finlay
First: 2025-06-16T05:43:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T05:42:19+00:00
Comments: The authors have determined that the current version contains incomplete analysis and preliminary results that are not suitable for public dissemination. The paper is withdrawn pending major revision
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper develops a novel multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) framework for reinsurance treaty bidding, addressing long-standing inefficiencies in traditional broker-mediated placement processes. We pose the core research question: Can autonomous, learning-based bidding systems improve risk transfer efficiency and outperform conventional pricing approaches in reinsurance markets? In our model, each reinsurer is represented by an adaptive agent that iteratively refines its bidding strategy within a competitive, partially observable environment. The simulation explicitly incorporates institutional frictions including broker intermediation, incumbent advantages, last-look privileges, and asymmetric access to underwriting information. Empirical analysis demonstrates that MARL agents achieve up to 15% higher underwriting profit, 20% lower tail risk (CVaR), and over 25% improvement in Sharpe ratios relative to actuarial and heuristic baselines. Sensitivity tests confirm robustness across hyperparameter settings, and stress testing reveals strong resilience under simulated catastrophe shocks and capital constraints. These findings suggest that MARL offers a viable path toward more transparent, adaptive, and risk-sensitive reinsurance markets. The proposed framework contributes to emerging literature at the intersection of algorithmic market design, strategic bidding, and AI-enabled financial decision-making.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于多智能体强化学习的动态再保险合约竞价研究
本文针对传统经纪中介安排流程中长期存在的效率低下问题，开发了一种创新的多智能体强化学习（MARL）框架用于再保险合约竞价。我们提出核心研究问题：在再保险市场中，基于学习的自主竞价系统能否提高风险转移效率并超越传统定价方法？ 在我们的模型中，每个再保险公司由一个自适应智能体代表，在竞争性、部分可观测的环境中迭代优化其竞价策略。该模拟明确纳入了机构摩擦因素，包括经纪中介、在位者优势、最后查看特权以及核保信息的不对称获取。 实证分析表明，相较于精算和启发式基准，MARL智能体可实现高达15%的核保利润提升、20%的尾部风险（CVaR）降低以及超过25%的夏普比率改善。敏感性测试证实了超参数设置下的稳健性，压力测试显示其在模拟巨灾冲击和资本约束下具有强大的韧性。 这些发现表明，MARL为构建更透明、自适应且风险敏感的再保险市场提供了可行路径。所提出的框架对算法市场设计、战略竞价和人工智能赋能金融决策交叉领域的新兴文献做出了贡献。

The method models each reinsurer as an agent operating in a competitive, partially observable environment that incorporates real-world frictions like broker intermediation and information asymmetry. Experimental results show that the MARL agents achieve up to 15% higher underwriting profit, 20% lower tail risk, and over 25% improvement in Sharpe ratios compared to conventional actuarial and heuristic baselines, demonstrating robustness in stress tests including simulated catastrophe shocks.
本文针对传统再保险条约经纪撮合过程中的低效问题，提出了一种多智能体强化学习框架，以实现再保险人之间的自主、自适应竞价。该方法将每个再保险人建模为在竞争性、部分可观测环境中运作的智能体，并纳入了经纪中介、信息不对称等现实摩擦。实验结果表明，与传统的精算和启发式基准相比，多智能体强化学习智能体实现了高达15%的更高承保利润、20%的更低保尾风险以及超过25%的夏普比率提升，在包括模拟巨灾冲击的压力测试中展现了稳健性。
Meta-Cognitive Reinforcement Learning with Self-Doubt and Recovery
Authors: Zhipeng Zhang, Xiongfei Su, Kai Li
First: 2026-01-28T02:43:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T05:08:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robust reinforcement learning methods typically focus on suppressing unreliable experiences or corrupted rewards, but they lack the ability to reason about the reliability of their own learning process. As a result, such methods often either overreact to noise by becoming overly conservative or fail catastrophically when uncertainty accumulates. In this work, we propose a meta-cognitive reinforcement learning framework that enables an agent to assess, regulate, and recover its learning behavior based on internally estimated reliability signals. The proposed method introduces a meta-trust variable driven by Value Prediction Error Stability (VPES), which modulates learning dynamics via fail-safe regulation and gradual trust recovery. Experiments on continuous-control benchmarks with reward corruption demonstrate that recovery-enabled meta-cognitive control achieves higher average returns and significantly reduces late-stage training failures compared to strong robustness baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自我怀疑与恢复的元认知强化学习
传统鲁棒强化学习方法通常侧重于抑制不可靠经验或受干扰奖励，但缺乏对自身学习过程可靠性的推理能力。这导致此类方法要么因过度保守而对噪声反应过激，要么在不确定性累积时发生灾难性失效。本研究提出一种元认知强化学习框架，使智能体能够基于内部估计的可靠性信号评估、调节并恢复其学习行为。该方法引入由价值预测误差稳定性驱动的元信任变量，通过故障安全调节与渐进信任恢复机制调控学习动态。在奖励受干扰的连续控制基准测试中，实验表明具备恢复能力的元认知控制相比强鲁棒基线方法，实现了更高的平均回报，并显著减少了训练后期的失效情况。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing robust reinforcement learning methods, which often become overly conservative or fail catastrophically due to an inability to reason about their own learning reliability, this paper proposes a meta-cognitive reinforcement learning framework. The method introduces a meta-trust variable driven by Value Prediction Error Stability (VPES) to enable the agent to assess, regulate, and recover its learning behavior through fail-safe regulation and gradual trust recovery. Experimental results on continuous-control benchmarks with reward corruption show that this recovery-enabled meta-cognitive control achieves higher average returns and significantly reduces late-stage training failures compared to strong robustness baselines.
现有鲁棒强化学习方法常因无法评估自身学习可靠性而变得过于保守或灾难性失败，为此本文提出一种元认知强化学习框架。该方法通过基于价值预测误差稳定性驱动的元信任变量，使智能体能够通过故障安全调节和渐进信任恢复来评估、调节和恢复其学习行为。在奖励被污染的连续控制基准测试中，实验结果表明，这种具备恢复能力的元认知控制相比强大的鲁棒性基线方法，实现了更高的平均回报并显著减少了训练后期的失败。
Adaptive Robust Estimator for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhongyi Li, Wan Tian, Jingyu Chen, Kangyao Huang, Huiming Zhang, Hui Yang, Tao Ren, Jinyang Jiang, Yijie Peng, Yikun Ban, Fuzhen Zhuang
First: 2026-03-23T04:51:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T04:51:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent collaboration has emerged as a powerful paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models, yet it suffers from interaction-level ambiguity that blurs generation, critique, and revision, making credit assignment across agents difficult. Moreover, policy optimization in this setting is vulnerable to heavy-tailed and noisy rewards, which can bias advantage estimation and trigger unstable or even divergent training. To address both issues, we propose a robust multi-agent reinforcement learning framework for collaborative reasoning, consisting of two components: Dual-Agent Answer-Critique-Rewrite (DACR) and an Adaptive Robust Estimator (ARE). DACR decomposes reasoning into a structured three-stage pipeline: answer, critique, and rewrite, while enabling explicit attribution of each agent's marginal contribution to its partner's performance. ARE provides robust estimation of batch experience means during multi-agent policy optimization. Across mathematical reasoning and embodied intelligence benchmarks, even under noisy rewards, our method consistently outperforms the baseline in both homogeneous and heterogeneous settings. These results indicate stronger robustness to reward noise and more stable training dynamics, effectively preventing optimization failures caused by noisy reward signals.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体强化学习的自适应鲁棒估计器
多智能体协作已成为增强大语言模型推理能力的有效范式，但其存在交互层面的模糊性，导致生成、批判与修订过程界限不清，难以实现跨智能体的贡献分配。此外，该场景下的策略优化易受重尾噪声奖励干扰，可能扭曲优势估计并引发训练不稳定甚至发散。为解决这两个问题，我们提出一个用于协作推理的鲁棒多智能体强化学习框架，包含双智能体应答-批判-重写模块与自适应鲁棒估计器两个核心组件。前者将推理过程解构为应答、批判、重写三阶段结构化流程，同时支持对每个智能体贡献度的显式归因；后者为多智能体策略优化提供批量经验均值的鲁棒估计。在数学推理与具身智能基准测试中，即使在噪声奖励环境下，本方法在同构与异构场景下均稳定优于基线模型。实验结果表明该方法对奖励噪声具有更强鲁棒性，训练动态更稳定，能有效避免噪声奖励信号导致的优化失效。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses two key challenges in multi-agent reinforcement learning for collaborative reasoning: ambiguous credit assignment due to interaction-level blurring and unstable training from heavy-tailed, noisy rewards. The proposed solution is a robust framework combining a Dual-Agent Answer-Critique-Rewrite (DACR) structure, which decomposes reasoning into distinct stages for clear contribution attribution, with an Adaptive Robust Estimator (ARE) to provide stable mean estimates during policy optimization. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning and embodied intelligence benchmarks demonstrate that the method outperforms baselines under noisy rewards in both homogeneous and heterogeneous settings, showing improved robustness to reward noise and more stable training dynamics that prevent optimization failures.
本文针对多智能体强化学习在协作推理中的两个关键挑战：交互模糊导致的信用分配困难，以及重尾噪声奖励引发的不稳定训练。提出的解决方案是一个鲁棒框架，结合了双智能体回答-批判-重写结构，将推理分解为明确阶段以实现贡献归因，以及自适应鲁棒估计器，用于在策略优化中提供稳定的经验均值估计。在数学推理和具身智能基准测试中，即使在噪声奖励下，该方法在同质和异质设置中均优于基线，表现出对奖励噪声更强的鲁棒性、更稳定的训练动态，有效防止了噪声信号导致的优化失败。
Counterfactual Credit Policy Optimization for Multi-Agent Collaboration
Authors: Zhongyi Li, Wan Tian, Yikun Ban, Jinju Chen, Huiming Zhang, Yang Liu, Fuzhen Zhuang
First: 2026-03-23T04:35:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T04:35:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Collaborative multi-agent large language models (LLMs) can solve complex reasoning tasks by decomposing roles and aggregating diverse hypotheses. Yet, reinforcement learning (RL) for such systems is often undermined by credit assignment: a shared global reward obscures individual contributions, inflating update variance and encouraging free-riding. We introduce Counterfactual Credit Policy Optimization (CCPO), a framework that assigns agent-specific learning signals by estimating each agent's marginal contribution through counterfactual trajectories. CCPO builds dynamic counterfactual baselines that simulate outcomes with an agent's contribution removed, yielding role-sensitive advantages for policy optimization. To further improve stability under heterogeneous tasks and data distributions, we propose a global-history-aware normalization scheme that calibrates advantages using global rollout statistics. We evaluate CCPO on two collaboration topologies: a sequential Think--Reason dyad and multi-agent voting. Across mathematical and logical reasoning benchmarks, CCPO mitigates free-riding and outperforms strong multi-agent RL baselines, yielding finer-grained and more effective credit assignment for collaborative LLM training. Our code is available at https://github.com/bhai114/ccpo.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多智能体协作的反事实信用策略优化
协作式多智能体大语言模型（LLM）可通过角色分解与多元假设聚合解决复杂推理任务。然而，此类系统的强化学习（RL）常受信用分配问题制约：共享的全局奖励模糊了个体贡献，增大了更新方差并诱发搭便车行为。本文提出反事实信用策略优化（CCPO）框架，通过反事实轨迹估计各智能体的边际贡献，从而分配智能体专属的学习信号。CCPO构建动态反事实基线，模拟移除特定智能体贡献后的结果，为策略优化生成角色敏感的优势函数。为提升异构任务与数据分布下的稳定性，我们进一步提出全局历史感知归一化方案，利用全局推演统计量校准优势函数。我们在两种协作拓扑结构（顺序型'思考-推理'双人组与多智能体投票）上评估CCPO。在数学与逻辑推理基准测试中，CCPO有效缓解搭便车现象，性能超越主流多智能体RL基线，为协作式LLM训练提供更细粒度、更高效的信用分配方案。代码已开源：https://github.com/bhai114/ccpo。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the credit assignment problem in reinforcement learning for collaborative multi-agent large language models, where a shared global reward obscures individual contributions and leads to high variance and free-riding. The authors propose Counterfactual Credit Policy Optimization (CCPO), a framework that assigns agent-specific learning signals by estimating each agent's marginal contribution through counterfactual trajectories, which simulate outcomes with an agent's contribution removed, and they enhance stability with a global-history-aware normalization scheme. Experimental results on mathematical and logical reasoning benchmarks with sequential and voting collaboration topologies show that CCPO mitigates free-riding and outperforms strong multi-agent RL baselines, enabling more effective credit assignment for collaborative training.
本文针对协作式多智能体大语言模型强化学习中的信用分配问题展开研究，该问题中共享的全局奖励掩盖了个体贡献，导致高方差和搭便车行为。作者提出了反事实信用策略优化框架，通过反事实轨迹估计每个智能体的边际贡献来分配个体学习信号，模拟去除智能体贡献后的结果，并采用全局历史感知的归一化方案提升稳定性。在数学和逻辑推理基准测试中，针对顺序和投票协作拓扑的实验结果表明，该框架有效缓解了搭便车现象，优于现有多智能体强化学习方法，实现了更精细有效的协作训练信用分配。
What Do World Models Learn in RL? Probing Latent Representations in Learned Environment Simulators
Authors: Xinyu Zhang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-23T04:00:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T04:00:53+00:00
Comments: 5 pages, 3 figures, 1 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
World models learn to simulate environment dynamics from experience, enabling sample-efficient reinforcement learning. But what do these models actually represent internally? We apply interpretability techniques--including linear and nonlinear probing, causal interventions, and attention analysis--to two architecturally distinct world models: IRIS (discrete token transformer) and DIAMOND (continuous diffusion UNet), trained on Atari Breakout and Pong. Using linear probes, we find that both models develop linearly decodable representations of game state variables (object positions, scores), with MLP probes yielding only marginally higher R^2, confirming that these representations are approximately linear. Causal interventions--shifting hidden states along probe-derived directions--produce correlated changes in model predictions, providing evidence that representations are functionally used rather than merely correlated. Analysis of IRIS attention heads reveals spatial specialization: specific heads attend preferentially to tokens overlapping with game objects. Multi-baseline token ablation experiments consistently identify object-containing tokens as disproportionately important. Our findings provide interpretability evidence that learned world models develop structured, approximately linear internal representations of environment state across two games and two architectures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中世界模型学习什么？探究习得环境模拟器的潜在表征
世界模型通过经验学习模拟环境动态，实现样本高效的强化学习。但这些模型内部实际表征了什么？我们应用可解释性技术——包括线性和非线性探针、因果干预及注意力分析——对两种架构不同的世界模型进行研究：在Atari Breakout和Pong上训练的IRIS（离散令牌变换器）与DIAMOND（连续扩散UNet）。通过线性探针发现，两种模型均形成游戏状态变量（物体位置、得分）的线性可解码表征，MLP探针仅略微提升R^2，证实这些表征近似线性。因果干预——沿探针推导方向偏移隐藏状态——引发模型预测的相关变化，证明表征具有功能效用而非仅相关性。IRIS注意力头分析显示空间特化：特定头部优先关注与游戏物体重叠的令牌。多基线令牌消融实验一致表明含物体令牌具有超比例重要性。研究结果为习得世界模型在两种游戏与架构中形成结构化、近似线性的环境状态内部表征提供了可解释性证据。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand what internal representations world models learn for sample-efficient reinforcement learning, this study applies interpretability techniques including linear and nonlinear probing, causal interventions, and attention analysis to two distinct architectures—IRIS (a discrete token transformer) and DIAMOND (a continuous diffusion UNet)—trained on Atari Breakout and Pong. The method reveals that both models develop linearly decodable representations of key game state variables such as object positions and scores, with only marginal improvements from nonlinear probes, indicating these representations are approximately linear. Experimental results show that causal interventions along probe-derived directions produce correlated changes in model predictions, demonstrating functional use of the representations, while attention analysis in IRIS identifies spatial specialization with specific heads attending to object-containing tokens, and token ablation experiments consistently highlight the importance of these tokens. These findings provide evidence that learned world models form structured, near-linear internal representations of environment state across different games and architectures.
本研究旨在探究世界模型在样本高效强化学习中学习到的内部表示，为此对两种不同架构——IRIS（离散令牌变换器）和DIAMOND（连续扩散UNet）——在Atari Breakout和Pong游戏上训练后，应用了包括线性和非线性探测、因果干预及注意力分析在内的可解释性技术。方法表明，两种模型都形成了对游戏状态变量（如物体位置和得分）的线性可解码表示，非线性探测仅带来边际改进，证实这些表示近似线性。实验结果中，沿探测方向进行因果干预会导致模型预测的相关变化，证明了表示的功能性使用；IRIS的注意力分析揭示了空间专门化，特定注意力头优先关注包含物体的令牌，而令牌消融实验一致识别出这些令牌的重要性。这些发现为世界模型在不同游戏和架构中形成结构化、近似线性的环境状态内部表示提供了可解释性证据。
Evolutionary Biparty Multiobjective UAV Path Planning: Problems and Empirical Comparisons
Authors: Kesheng Chen, Wenjian Luo, Xin Lin, Zhen Song, Yatong Chang
Venue: Chen, K., Luo, W., Lin, X., Song, Z., & Chang, Y. (2024). Evolutionary biparty multiobjective UAV path planning: Problems and empirical comparisons. IEEE Transactions on Emerging Topics in Computational Intelligence, 8(3), 2433-2445
First: 2026-03-23T03:57:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T03:57:51+00:00
Comments: \c{opyright} 2026 IEEE. Personal use of this material is permitted. Permission from IEEE must be obtained for all other uses, in any current or future media, including reprinting/republishing this material for advertising or promotional purposes, creating new collective works, for resale or redistribution to servers or lists, or reuse of any copyrighted component of this work in other works
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) have been widely used in urban missions, and proper planning of UAV paths can improve mission efficiency while reducing the risk of potential third-party impact. Existing work has considered all efficiency and safety objectives for a single decision-maker (DM) and regarded this as a multiobjective optimization problem (MOP). However, there is usually not a single DM but two DMs, i.e., an efficiency DM and a safety DM, and the DMs are only concerned with their respective objectives. The final decision is made based on the solutions of both DMs. In this paper, for the first time, biparty multiobjective UAV path planning (BPMO-UAVPP) problems involving both efficiency and safety departments are modeled. The existing multiobjective immune algorithm with nondominated neighbor-based selection (NNIA), the hybrid evolutionary framework for the multiobjective immune algorithm (HEIA), and the adaptive immune-inspired multiobjective algorithm (AIMA) are modified for solving the BPMO-UAVPP problem, and then biparty multiobjective optimization algorithms, including the BPNNIA, BPHEIA, and BPAIMA, are proposed and comprehensively compared with traditional multiobjective evolutionary algorithms and typical multiparty multiobjective evolutionary algorithms (i.e., OptMPNDS and OptMPNDS2). The experimental results show that BPAIMA performs better than ordinary multiobjective evolutionary algorithms such as NSGA-II and multiparty multiobjective evolutionary algorithms such as OptMPNDS, OptMPNDS2, BPNNIA and BPHEIA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：进化双部门多目标无人机路径规划：问题与实证比较
无人机已广泛应用于城市任务，合理的路径规划能提升任务效率并降低潜在第三方影响风险。现有研究将所有效率与安全目标视为单一决策者的多目标优化问题，但实际通常存在两个决策部门——效率部门与安全部门，各自仅关注其目标，最终决策需综合双方方案。本文首次建立了涉及效率与安全部门的双部门多目标无人机路径规划问题模型，通过改进现有非支配邻域选择多目标免疫算法、混合进化免疫算法框架及自适应免疫多目标算法，提出了BPNNIA、BPHEIA和BPAIMA三种双部门多目标优化算法，并与传统多目标进化算法及典型多方多目标进化算法（OptMPNDS与OptMPNDS2）进行全面对比。实验表明，BPAIMA在性能上优于NSGA-II等普通多目标进化算法，以及OptMPNDS、OptMPNDS2、BPNNIA和BPHEIA等多方多目标进化算法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the need for more realistic decision-making in UAV path planning by modeling it as a biparty multiobjective optimization problem (BPMO-UAVPP), where separate efficiency and safety decision-makers each prioritize their own objectives before a joint final decision. The method modifies existing multiobjective immune algorithms (NNIA, HEIA, AIMA) to create three new biparty algorithms—BPNNIA, BPHEIA, and BPAIMA—and compares them against traditional and multiparty evolutionary algorithms. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed BPAIMA outperforms both standard multiobjective algorithms like NSGA-II and other multiparty approaches, including OptMPNDS, OptMPNDS2, BPNNIA, and BPHEIA.
本文针对无人机路径规划中更现实的决策需求，将其建模为一个双部门多目标优化问题（BPMO-UAVPP），其中效率和安全两个决策部门分别关注各自目标，再共同做出最终决策。方法上，通过改进现有的多目标免疫算法（如NNIA、HEIA、AIMA），提出了三种新的双部门算法——BPNNIA、BPHEIA和BPAIMA，并与传统多目标进化算法及典型多部门算法（如OptMPNDS、OptMPNDS2）进行了比较。实验结果表明，所提出的BPAIMA在性能上优于NSGA-II等普通多目标算法，也优于OptMPNDS、OptMPNDS2、BPNNIA和BPHEIA等其他多部门算法。
BOxCrete: A Bayesian Optimization Open-Source AI Model for Concrete Strength Forecasting and Mix Optimization
Authors: Bayezid Baten, M. Ayyan Iqbal, Sebastian Ament, Julius Kusuma, Nishant Garg
First: 2026-03-23T03:33:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T03:33:40+00:00
Comments: Code and dataset are available at https://github.com/facebookresearch/SustainableConcrete
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Modern concrete must simultaneously satisfy evolving demands for mechanical performance, workability, durability, and sustainability, making mix designs increasingly complex. Recent studies leveraging Artificial Intelligence (AI) and Machine Learning (ML) models show promise for predicting compressive strength and guiding mix optimization, but most existing efforts are based on proprietary industrial datasets and closed-source implementations. Here we introduce BOxCrete, an open-source probabilistic modeling and optimization framework trained on a new open-access dataset of over 500 strength measurements (1-15 ksi) from 123 mixtures - 69 mortar and 54 concrete mixes tested at five curing ages (1, 3, 5, 14, and 28 days). BOxCrete leverages Gaussian Process (GP) regression to predict strength development, achieving average R$^2$ = 0.94 and RMSE = 0.69 ksi, quantify uncertainty, and carry out multi-objective optimization of compressive strength and embodied carbon. The dataset and model establish a reproducible open-source foundation for data-driven development of AI-based optimized mix designs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BOxCrete：用于混凝土强度预测与配合比优化的贝叶斯优化开源人工智能模型
现代混凝土需同时满足力学性能、工作性、耐久性与可持续性等动态需求，导致配合比设计日益复杂。近期利用人工智能与机器学习模型的研究在预测抗压强度与指导配合比优化方面展现出潜力，但现有成果多基于专有工业数据集与闭源实现。本文提出BOxCrete——一个基于新建开放数据集训练的开源概率建模与优化框架，该数据集涵盖123种混合料（69种砂浆与54种混凝土）在五个养护龄期（1、3、5、14、28天）测试获得的500余组强度测量值（1-15 ksi）。BOxCrete采用高斯过程回归预测强度发展，平均R²=0.94、RMSE=0.69 ksi，可量化不确定性并执行抗压强度与隐含碳排放的多目标优化。该数据集与模型为基于人工智能的优化配合比设计建立了可复现的开源数据驱动基础。

The motivation for this work is to address the growing complexity of modern concrete mix design, which must balance performance, workability, durability, and sustainability, while overcoming the limitations of prior AI/ML approaches that often rely on proprietary data and closed-source tools. The method introduces BOxCrete, an open-source Bayesian optimization framework that uses Gaussian Process regression trained on a new open-access dataset of over 500 strength measurements from 123 mortar and concrete mixes across five curing ages. The main experimental results show that the model achieves high predictive accuracy with an average R² of 0.94 and RMSE of 0.69 ksi, effectively quantifies uncertainty, and enables multi-objective optimization of compressive strength and embodied carbon, providing a reproducible foundation for AI-driven mix design.
