Learning to Reason without External Rewards
Authors: Xuandong Zhao, Zhewei Kang, Aosong Feng, Sergey Levine, Dawn Song
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-26T07:01:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T03:10:39+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Training large language models (LLMs) for complex reasoning via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) is effective but limited by reliance on costly, domain-specific supervision. We explore Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF), a framework that enables LLMs to learn from intrinsic signals without external rewards or labeled data. We propose Intuitor, an RLIF method that uses a model's own confidence-termed self-certainty-as its sole reward signal. Intuitor replaces external rewards in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with self-certainty scores, enabling fully unsupervised learning. Experiments demonstrate that Intuitor matches GRPO's performance on mathematical benchmarks while achieving better generalization to out-of-domain tasks like code generation, without requiring gold solutions or test cases. Our findings show that intrinsic model signals can drive effective learning across domains, offering a scalable alternative to RLVR for autonomous AI systems where verifiable rewards are unavailable. Code is available at https://github.com/sunblaze-ucb/Intuitor
中文标题/摘要
标题：无需外部奖励的推理学习
通过可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）训练大型语言模型（LLM）进行复杂推理虽然有效，但受限于对昂贵领域特定监督的依赖。我们探索了内部反馈强化学习（RLIF），该框架使LLM能够从内在信号中学习，无需外部奖励或标注数据。我们提出Intuitor方法，该方法以模型自身置信度（称为自我确定性）作为唯一奖励信号。Intuitor将组相对策略优化（GRPO）中的外部奖励替换为自我确定性分数，实现完全无监督学习。实验表明，Intuitor在数学基准测试中达到与GRPO相当的性能，同时在代码生成等跨领域任务上实现更好的泛化能力，且无需标准答案或测试用例。我们的研究证明，内在模型信号能够驱动跨领域有效学习，为缺乏可验证奖励的自主AI系统提供了可扩展的RLVR替代方案。代码发布于https://github.com/sunblaze-ucb/Intuitor
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), which requires costly external supervision, by proposing Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF) to enable large language models to learn from intrinsic signals without external rewards or labeled data. The method introduces Intuitor, which uses a model's own confidence, termed self-certainty, as the sole reward signal within the Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) framework, allowing for fully unsupervised learning. Experimental results show that Intuitor matches GRPO's performance on mathematical benchmarks and achieves better generalization to out-of-domain tasks like code generation, without needing gold solutions or test cases, demonstrating that intrinsic signals can drive effective learning across domains and offer a scalable alternative to RLVR for autonomous AI systems.
本文针对依赖外部监督且成本高昂的强化学习与可验证奖励方法，提出了强化学习内部反馈框架，使大语言模型能够无需外部奖励或标注数据，仅从内在信号中学习。该方法引入了Intuitor，利用模型自身的置信度作为唯一奖励信号，结合群体相对策略优化框架，实现了完全无监督学习。实验结果表明，Intuitor在数学基准测试中与群体相对策略优化表现相当，并在代码生成等域外任务上实现了更好的泛化能力，无需黄金解决方案或测试用例，证明了内在信号能驱动跨领域有效学习，为自主人工智能系统提供了一种可扩展的替代方案。
Formula-R1: Incentivizing LLM Reasoning over Complex Tables with Numerical Computation via Formula-Driven Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lang Cao, Jingxian Xu, Hanbing Liu, Jinyu Wang, Mengyu Zhou, Haoyu Dong, Shi Han, Dongmei Zhang
First: 2025-05-29T17:13:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T03:07:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tables are a fundamental medium for organizing and analyzing data, making table reasoning a critical capability for intelligent systems. Although large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong general reasoning abilities, they still struggle with accurate numerical reasoning over tabular data, particularly in complex table settings beyond simple relational lookup. Spreadsheet formulas provide a powerful and expressive interface for executable symbolic operations, enabling rich reasoning patterns that remain largely underexplored by existing LLMs. In this paper, we introduce Formula-R1, a model trained via Formula Tuning (Fortune), a formula-driven reinforcement learning (RL) framework for table reasoning. Formula Tuning trains LLMs to generate executable spreadsheet formulas for question answering over general tabular data, using execution success and answer correctness as reward signals, thereby reducing reliance on supervised formula annotations. We demonstrate the effectiveness of Formula Tuning through extensive experiments on seven table reasoning benchmarks. It substantially improves LLM performance on table reasoning, particularly for tasks involving complex tables and multi-step numerical computation. Moreover, Formula-R1 consistently outperforms prior methods under controlled comparison settings. Beyond empirical gains, our extensive analyses provide insights into the role of RL in formula-driven table reasoning, highlighting the broader potential of formula-driven RL to enhance reasoning capabilities in LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Formula-R1：通过公式驱动强化学习激励大语言模型对复杂表格进行数值计算推理
表格是组织和分析数据的基本媒介，使表格推理成为智能系统的关键能力。尽管大语言模型展现出强大的通用推理能力，但在处理表格数据的精确数值推理方面仍存在困难，尤其是在超越简单关系查找的复杂表格场景中。电子表格公式为可执行的符号操作提供了强大且富有表现力的接口，能够实现丰富的推理模式，而现有大语言模型对此尚未充分探索。本文提出Formula-R1模型，该模型通过公式调优进行训练——这是一种用于表格推理的公式驱动强化学习框架。公式调优训练大语言模型为通用表格数据的问答生成可执行的电子表格公式，以执行成功率和答案正确性作为奖励信号，从而减少对监督式公式标注的依赖。我们在七个表格推理基准测试中通过大量实验验证了公式调优的有效性。该方法显著提升了大语言模型在表格推理方面的性能，特别是在涉及复杂表格和多步数值计算的任务中。此外，在受控对比环境下，Formula-R1始终优于现有方法。除实证成果外，我们的深入分析揭示了强化学习在公式驱动表格推理中的作用，彰显了公式驱动强化学习在增强大语言模型推理能力方面的广阔潜力。

Learning Can Converge Stably to the Wrong Belief under Latent Reliability
Authors: Zhipeng Zhang, Zhenjie Yao, Kai Li, Lei Yang
First: 2026-03-23T02:28:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T02:28:07+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 6 figures. Extended and refocused version of arXiv:2601.09261
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning systems are typically optimized by minimizing loss or maximizing reward, assuming that improvements in these signals reflect progress toward the true objective. However, when feedback reliability is unobservable, this assumption can fail, and learning algorithms may converge stably to incorrect solutions. This failure arises because single-step feedback does not reveal whether an experience is informative or persistently biased. When information is aggregated over learning trajectories, however, systematic differences between reliable and unreliable regimes can emerge. We propose a Monitor-Trust-Regulator (MTR) framework that infers reliability from learning dynamics and modulates updates through a slow-timescale trust variable. Across reinforcement learning and supervised learning settings, standard algorithms exhibit stable optimization behavior while learning incorrect solutions under latent unreliability, whereas trust-modulated systems reduce bias accumulation and improve recovery. These results suggest that learning dynamics are not only optimization traces but also a source of information about feedback reliability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：潜在可靠性下学习可能稳定收敛至错误信念
学习系统通常通过最小化损失或最大化奖励进行优化，其假设是这些信号的改进反映了向真实目标的进展。然而，当反馈可靠性不可观测时，这一假设可能失效，学习算法可能稳定收敛至错误解。这种失败源于单步反馈无法揭示经验是否具有信息性或存在持续偏差。但当信息在学习轨迹上聚合时，可靠与不可靠机制间的系统性差异便会显现。我们提出了监控-信任-调节器框架，该框架从学习动态推断可靠性，并通过慢时标信任变量调节更新。在强化学习和监督学习场景中，标准算法在潜在不可靠条件下学习错误解时仍表现出稳定优化行为，而信任调节系统则能减少偏差累积并提升恢复能力。这些结果表明学习动态不仅是优化轨迹，也是反馈可靠性的信息来源。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that standard learning algorithms, which optimize based on feedback signals like loss or reward, can stably converge to incorrect solutions when feedback reliability is latent and unobservable, as single-step feedback fails to distinguish informative from biased experiences. To address this, the authors propose the Monitor-Trust-Regulator (MTR) framework, which infers reliability from learning dynamics over trajectories and modulates updates using a slow-timescale trust variable. Experimental results in reinforcement and supervised learning settings show that standard algorithms exhibit stable optimization but learn wrong beliefs under latent unreliability, while trust-modulated systems reduce bias accumulation and improve recovery, indicating that learning dynamics provide valuable information about feedback reliability.
本文的动机在于观察到标准学习算法基于损失或奖励等反馈信号进行优化时，若反馈可靠性是潜在且不可观测的，可能稳定地收敛到错误解，因为单步反馈无法区分信息性经验与持续偏见。为解决此问题，作者提出了监控-信任-调节器（MTR）框架，该框架从学习轨迹的动态中推断可靠性，并通过慢时间尺度的信任变量调节更新。在强化学习和监督学习设置中的实验结果表明，标准算法在潜在不可靠性下表现出稳定优化但学习到错误信念，而信任调节系统减少了偏差累积并改善了恢复能力，这表明学习动态提供了关于反馈可靠性的重要信息。
RadHiera: Semantic Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning for Medical Report Generation
Authors: Bodong Du, Honglong Yang, Xiaomeng Li
First: 2025-11-13T08:10:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T01:46:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-language models have shown promising results in radiology report generation. However, most existing methods generate reports as flat text and do not explicitly model the semantic dependency between the Findings and Impression sections, which can lead to inconsistencies between clinical observations and diagnostic conclusions. In this paper, we propose RadHiera, a semantic hierarchical reinforcement learning framework for radiology report generation. RadHiera follows the semantic organization of radiology reports by first optimizing overall report quality, then improving the diagnostic accuracy of the Impression section, and finally enforcing consistency between Findings and Impression so that diagnostic conclusions are supported by clinical evidence. Specifically, we begin with a base reward that combines linguistic quality and medical factuality to provide supervision on the whole report. On this basis, we introduce a severity-aware reward for the Impression section that places greater emphasis on errors involving clinically critical conditions, thereby reducing both missed diagnoses and overstatement. We further enforce cross-section consistency using Expert Model-derived label sets, with subset constraints and hallucination penalties to ensure that impressions remain faithful to the findings. Experiments on three public chest X-ray benchmarks show that RadHiera consistently improves diagnostic accuracy and inter-section consistency over state-of-the-art methods, while also demonstrating good adaptability to report generation in ultrasound report generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RadHiera：用于医学报告生成的语义分层强化学习
视觉语言模型在放射学报告生成中已展现出有前景的结果。然而，现有方法大多将报告生成为扁平文本，未显式建模“发现”与“印象”部分间的语义依赖关系，可能导致临床观察与诊断结论不一致。本文提出RadHiera，一种用于放射学报告生成的语义分层强化学习框架。RadHiera遵循放射学报告的语义组织方式：先优化整体报告质量，再提升“印象”部分的诊断准确性，最后强化“发现”与“印象”间的一致性，使诊断结论得到临床证据支持。具体而言，我们首先采用结合语言质量与医学事实性的基础奖励函数监督整份报告；在此基础上，为“印象”部分引入严重性感知奖励，更侧重涉及临床关键状况的错误，从而减少漏诊与过度诊断；进一步通过专家模型衍生的标签集，结合子集约束与幻觉惩罚机制，确保印象部分忠实于发现内容。在三个公开胸部X光基准上的实验表明，RadHiera在诊断准确性与跨部分一致性上持续优于现有先进方法，同时在超声报告生成任务中也展现出良好适应性。

Conformal Constrained Policy Optimization for Cost-Effective LLM Agents
Authors: Wenwen Si, Sooyong Jang, Insup Lee, Osbert Bastani
First: 2025-11-14T19:39:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T01:39:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While large language models (LLMs) have recently made tremendous progress towards solving challenging AI problems, they have done so at increasingly steep computational and API costs. We propose a novel strategy where we combine multiple LLM models with varying cost/accuracy tradeoffs in an agentic manner, where models and tools are run in sequence as determined by an orchestration model to minimize cost subject to a user-specified level of reliability; this constraint is formalized using conformal prediction to provide guarantees. To solve this problem, we propose Conformal Constrained Policy Optimization (CCPO), a training paradigm that integrates constrained policy optimization with off-policy reinforcement learning and recent advances in online conformal prediction. CCPO jointly optimizes a cost-aware policy (score function) and an adaptive threshold. Across two multi-hop question answering benchmarks, CCPO achieves up to a 30% cost reduction compared to other cost-aware baselines and LLM-guided methods without compromising reliability. Our approach provides a principled and practical framework for deploying LLM agents that are significantly more cost-effective while maintaining reliability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向成本效益型大语言模型智能体的保形约束策略优化
尽管大语言模型（LLMs）近期在解决复杂人工智能问题上取得显著进展，但其计算与API调用成本也急剧攀升。本文提出一种创新策略：以智能体形式整合多个具备不同成本/精度权衡特性的LLM模型，通过编排模型按序调度模型与工具，在满足用户指定可靠性水平的前提下实现成本最小化——该约束通过保形预测方法形式化以保证性能。为此，我们提出保形约束策略优化（CCPO），该训练范式将约束策略优化、离轨强化学习及在线保形预测的最新进展相结合。CCPO联合优化成本感知策略（评分函数）与自适应阈值。在两个多跳问答基准测试中，CCPO在保持可靠性的前提下，相较其他成本感知基线方法与LLM引导方法，最高可实现30%的成本降低。本方法为部署大语言模型智能体提供了兼具理论原则与实践价值的框架，在保障可靠性的同时显著提升成本效益。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the steep computational and API costs of deploying large language models (LLMs) for complex tasks, this paper introduces a strategy to combine multiple LLMs with varying cost-accuracy tradeoffs in an agentic sequence orchestrated to minimize cost while guaranteeing a user-specified reliability level, formalized via conformal prediction. The method, Conformal Constrained Policy Optimization (CCPO), integrates constrained policy optimization with off-policy reinforcement learning and online conformal prediction to jointly optimize a cost-aware policy and an adaptive threshold. Experimental results on two multi-hop question answering benchmarks show that CCPO achieves up to a 30% cost reduction compared to other cost-aware and LLM-guided baselines without compromising reliability, offering a principled framework for cost-effective LLM agent deployment.
本文的动机是应对大型语言模型（LLM）在解决复杂任务时日益增长的计算和API成本，提出了一种策略，将多个具有不同成本-精度权衡的LLM以智能体序列方式组合，通过编排模型顺序运行来最小化成本，同时利用符合预测来形式化保证用户指定的可靠性水平。方法上，提出了符合约束策略优化（CCPO），它将约束策略优化与离策略强化学习及在线符合预测相结合，共同优化成本感知策略和自适应阈值。在两个多跳问答基准上的主要实验结果表明，CCPO在不损害可靠性的前提下，相比其他成本感知基线和LLM引导方法，实现了高达30%的成本降低，为部署成本效益高的LLM智能体提供了一个原则性实用框架。
DRTriton: Large-Scale Synthetic Data Reinforcement Learning for Triton Kernel Generation
Authors: Siqi Guo, Ming Lin, Tianbao Yang
First: 2026-03-23T00:59:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T00:59:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Developing efficient CUDA kernels is a fundamental yet challenging task in the generative AI industry. Recent researches leverage Large Language Models (LLMs) to automatically convert PyTorch reference implementations to CUDA kernels, significantly reducing the engineering efforts. State-of-the-art LLMs, such as GPT-5.2 and Claude-Sonnet-4.5, still struggle in this specific task. To address this challenge, we propose DRTriton, a scalable learning framework for training LLMs to convert PyTorch codes into highly optimized Triton kernels, which are then compiled to CUDA kernels at runtime. DRTriton consists of three key components: (i) a data synthetic algorithm CSP-DAG that guarantees full coverage and unbiased uniform sampling over the operator space with controlled difficulty; (ii) a curriculum reinforcement learning with decoupled reward efficiently optimizes conversion success rate and inference speed simultaneously; and (iii) a test-time search algorithm that further improves the inference speed of the generated Triton kernels. Notably, despite being trained exclusively on synthetic data, DRTriton generalizes effectively to real-world CUDA kernels that are challenging even for human experts. Experimental results show that DRTriton-7B achieves speedup on 92% of the KernelBench Level 2, compared to 23% for GPT-5.2 and 19% for Claude-Sonnet-4.5.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DRTriton：面向Triton内核生成的大规模合成数据强化学习框架
开发高效的CUDA内核是生成式AI领域基础且具有挑战性的任务。近期研究利用大语言模型（LLM）自动将PyTorch参考实现转换为CUDA内核，显著降低了工程成本。然而，GPT-5.2和Claude-Sonnet-4.5等前沿LLM在此特定任务中仍存在困难。为此，我们提出DRTriton——一个可扩展的学习框架，通过训练LLM将PyTorch代码转换为高度优化的Triton内核（运行时编译为CUDA内核）。该框架包含三大核心组件：（1）CSP-DAG数据合成算法，可在控制难度条件下实现算子空间的完全覆盖与无偏均匀采样；（2）解耦奖励的课程强化学习，同步优化转换成功率和推理速度；（3）测试时搜索算法，进一步提升生成Triton内核的推理速度。值得注意的是，尽管仅使用合成数据训练，DRTriton能有效泛化至对人类专家都极具挑战的真实CUDA内核。实验表明：在KernelBench Level 2测试集上，DRTriton-7B在92%的案例中实现加速，而GPT-5.2和Claude-Sonnet-4.5的加速比例分别为23%和19%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind DRTriton is to automate the conversion of PyTorch code into highly optimized CUDA kernels, a task that remains difficult even for advanced large language models like GPT-5.2 and Claude-Sonnet-4.5. The method introduces a scalable framework that first uses a synthetic data generation algorithm, CSP-DAG, to create diverse and uniformly sampled operator examples, then applies curriculum reinforcement learning with decoupled rewards to simultaneously improve conversion success and kernel speed, and finally employs a test-time search to further optimize inference performance. Experimental results demonstrate strong generalization to real-world kernels, with the 7B parameter model achieving speedups on 92% of the KernelBench Level 2 benchmarks, significantly outperforming the compared LLMs.
DRTriton的研发动机是自动化将PyTorch代码转换为高度优化的CUDA内核，这一任务即使对于GPT-5.2和Claude-Sonnet-4.5等先进大语言模型仍具挑战。该方法提出了一个可扩展的学习框架：首先通过CSP-DAG合成数据算法生成覆盖全面、难度可控的算子样本；随后采用解耦奖励的课程强化学习，同步优化转换成功率和推理速度；最后通过测试时搜索算法进一步提成生成的Triton内核性能。实验结果表明，尽管仅使用合成数据训练，该模型能有效泛化至现实世界中专家也难处理的CUDA内核，其70亿参数版本在KernelBench Level 2测试集上实现了92%的加速覆盖率，显著优于对比模型。
KG-Hopper: Empowering Compact Open LLMs with Knowledge Graph Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shuai Wang, Yinan Yu
First: 2026-03-22T23:07:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-22T23:07:29+00:00
Comments: Accepted to IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate impressive natural language capabilities but often struggle with knowledge-intensive reasoning tasks. Knowledge Base Question Answering (KBQA), which leverages structured Knowledge Graphs (KGs) exemplifies this challenge due to the need for accurate multi-hop reasoning. Existing approaches typically perform sequential reasoning steps guided by predefined pipelines, restricting flexibility and causing error cascades due to isolated reasoning at each step. To address these limitations, we propose KG-Hopper, a novel Reinforcement Learning (RL) framework that empowers compact open LLMs with the ability to perform integrated multi-hop KG reasoning within a single inference round. Rather than reasoning step-by-step, we train a Reasoning LLM that embeds the entire KG traversal and decision process into a unified ``thinking'' stage, enabling global reasoning over cross-step dependencies and dynamic path exploration with backtracking. Experimental results on eight KG reasoning benchmarks show that KG-Hopper, based on a 7B-parameter LLM, consistently outperforms larger multi-step systems (up to 70B) and achieves competitive performance with proprietary models such as GPT-3.5-Turbo and GPT-4o-mini, while remaining compact, open, and data-efficient. The code is publicly available at: https://github.com/Wangshuaiia/KG-Hopper.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KG-Hopper：通过强化学习赋能紧凑型开源大语言模型实现知识图谱推理
大语言模型（LLMs）在自然语言处理方面展现出卓越能力，但在知识密集型推理任务中常面临挑战。以结构化知识图谱（KGs）为基础的知识库问答（KBQA）任务因需进行精确的多跳推理而凸显了这一难题。现有方法通常依赖预定义流程执行顺序推理步骤，这种分步独立推理的方式限制了灵活性并易导致错误级联。为突破这些局限，我们提出KG-Hopper——一种新颖的强化学习（RL）框架，使紧凑型开源LLMs能够在单轮推理中完成集成式多跳知识图谱推理。我们训练了一个推理大语言模型，将完整的图谱遍历与决策过程嵌入统一的“思考”阶段，而非逐步推理，从而实现对跨步骤依赖的全局推理及具备回溯能力的动态路径探索。在八个知识图谱推理基准测试中，基于70亿参数LLM的KG-Hopper持续超越规模更大的多步推理系统（最高达700亿参数），并与GPT-3.5-Turbo、GPT-4o-mini等专有模型达到相当性能，同时保持紧凑、开源和数据高效的特点。代码已开源：https://github.com/Wangshuaiia/KG-Hopper。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of enabling compact open LLMs to perform complex knowledge graph reasoning, as they often struggle with multi-hop tasks like KBQA where existing step-by-step methods are inflexible and error-prone. The proposed method, KG-Hopper, introduces a reinforcement learning framework that trains a Reasoning LLM to integrate the entire KG traversal and decision process into a single unified thinking stage, allowing for global reasoning with backtracking and dynamic path exploration. Experimental results on eight benchmarks demonstrate that KG-Hopper, using a 7B-parameter LLM, outperforms larger multi-step systems up to 70B parameters and achieves competitive performance with proprietary models like GPT-3.5-Turbo and GPT-4o-mini, while remaining compact and data-efficient.
该论文旨在解决紧凑型开源大语言模型在知识图谱推理任务中的挑战，因为现有分步方法在知识库问答等多跳推理中不够灵活且容易出错。提出的方法KG-Hopper采用强化学习框架，训练一个推理大语言模型，将整个知识图谱遍历和决策过程整合到统一的“思考”阶段，支持全局推理、回溯和动态路径探索。在八个基准测试上的实验结果表明，基于7B参数大语言模型的KG-Hopper性能优于高达70B参数的多步系统，并与GPT-3.5-Turbo和GPT-4o-mini等专有模型竞争，同时保持紧凑和数据高效。
PivotRL: High Accuracy Agentic Post-Training at Low Compute Cost
Authors: Junkeun Yi, Damon Mosk-Aoyama, Baihe Huang, Ritu Gala, Charles Wang, Sugam Dipak Devare, Khushi Bhardwaj, Abhibha Gupta, Oleksii Kuchaiev, Jiantao Jiao, Jian Zhang, Venkat Srinivasan
First: 2026-03-22T19:59:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-22T19:59:48+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 5 figures, 6 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training for long-horizon agentic tasks has a tension between compute efficiency and generalization. While supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is compute efficient, it often suffers from out-of-domain (OOD) degradation. Conversely, end-to-end reinforcement learning (E2E RL) preserves OOD capabilities, but incurs high compute costs due to many turns of on-policy rollout. We introduce PivotRL, a novel framework that operates on existing SFT trajectories to combine the compute efficiency of SFT with the OOD accuracy of E2E RL. PivotRL relies on two key mechanisms: first, it executes local, on-policy rollouts and filters for pivots: informative intermediate turns where sampled actions exhibit high variance in outcomes; second, it utilizes rewards for functional-equivalent actions rather than demanding strict string matching with the SFT data demonstration. We theoretically show that these mechanisms incentivize strong learning signals with high natural gradient norm, while maximally preserving policy probability ordering on actions unrelated to training tasks. In comparison to standard SFT on identical data, we demonstrate that PivotRL achieves +4.17% higher in-domain accuracy on average across four agentic domains, and +10.04% higher OOD accuracy in non-agentic tasks. Notably, on agentic coding tasks, PivotRL achieves competitive accuracy with E2E RL with 4x fewer rollout turns. PivotRL is adopted by NVIDIA's Nemotron-3-Super-120B-A12B, acting as the workhorse in production-scale agentic post-training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PivotRL：以低计算成本实现高精度智能体后训练
面向长周期智能体任务的后训练存在计算效率与泛化能力之间的权衡。监督微调（SFT）计算效率高，但常受域外（OOD）性能退化影响；端到端强化学习（E2E RL）虽能保持OOD能力，却因需多轮同策略推演而产生高昂计算成本。本文提出PivotRL框架，基于现有SFT轨迹，融合SFT的计算效率与E2E RL的OOD精度。其核心机制包括：1）执行局部同策略推演并筛选关键转折点——即采样行动在结果中呈现高方差的强信息性中间步骤；2）采用功能等价行动奖励机制，而非强制要求与SFT演示数据严格字符串匹配。理论证明该机制能激励具有高自然梯度范数的强学习信号，同时最大限度保持与训练任务无关行动的策略概率顺序。实验表明，在相同数据上，PivotRL在四个智能体领域的平均域内准确率较标准SFT提升4.17%，在非智能体任务的OOD准确率提升10.04%。在智能体编码任务中，PivotRL仅用E2E RL四分之一推演轮数即达到同等精度。该技术已被英伟达Nemotron-3-Super-120B-A12B模型采用，成为生产级智能体后训练的核心方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces PivotRL, a framework designed to address the trade-off between compute efficiency and out-of-domain generalization in post-training for agentic tasks. The method leverages existing supervised fine-tuning trajectories by identifying pivotal turns with high outcome variance for local on-policy rollouts and using rewards based on functional equivalence rather than exact string matching. Experimental results show that PivotRL improves in-domain accuracy by +4.17% and out-of-domain accuracy by +10.04% compared to standard supervised fine-tuning, while achieving competitive performance with end-to-end reinforcement learning using four times fewer rollout turns, as demonstrated in agentic coding tasks and adopted in NVIDIA's Nemotron-3 model.
本文提出了PivotRL框架，旨在解决智能体任务后训练中计算效率与跨域泛化能力之间的权衡问题。该方法利用现有的监督微调轨迹，通过识别结果方差高的关键转折点进行局部策略滚动，并采用基于功能等效而非严格字符串匹配的奖励机制。实验结果表明，与标准监督微调相比，PivotRL在四个智能体领域平均提升域内准确率4.17%，在非智能体任务中提升跨域准确率10.04%，且在智能体编程任务中以四倍更少的滚动轮次达到与端到端强化学习相竞争的性能，已被英伟达Nemotron-3模型采用于生产级智能体后训练。
